# 

<span key="07ef07616e144830b443a57dae05c195"><span offset-key="07ef07616e144830b443a57dae05c195:0">All About Scope</span></span>

<span key="2dd0693d07014ee786c156b24f89a901"><span offset-key="2dd0693d07014ee786c156b24f89a901:0">The </span>**scope**<span offset-key="2dd0693d07014ee786c156b24f89a901:2"> of a program in JavaScript is the set of variables that are available for use within the program. If a variable or other expression is not in the current scope, then it is unavailable for use. If we declare a variable, this variable will only be valid in the scope where we declared it. We can have nested scopes, but we'll see that in a little bit.</span></span>

<span key="a4e00dd52587406abac2bd226e60a20c"><span offset-key="a4e00dd52587406abac2bd226e60a20c:0">When we declare a variable in a certain scope, it will evaluate to a specific value </span>**in that scope**<span offset-key="a4e00dd52587406abac2bd226e60a20c:2">. We have been using the concept of scope in our code all along! Now we are just giving this concept a name.</span></span>

<span key="78d8964f18b446df9999676cc0462760"><span offset-key="78d8964f18b446df9999676cc0462760:0">By the end of this reading you should be able to predict the evaluation of code that utilizes local scope, block scope, lexical scope, and scope chaining</span></span>

## 

<span key="874d5e8e510846d4a87a7957661d7f64"><span offset-key="874d5e8e510846d4a87a7957661d7f64:0">Advantages of utilizing scope</span></span>

<span key="36477e43872348acbd2bc6b5f454278d"><span offset-key="36477e43872348acbd2bc6b5f454278d:0">Before we start talking about different types of scope we'll be talking about the two main advantages that scope gives us:</span></span>

1.  <span class="r-1awozwy r-1nf4jbm r-6koalj r-18u37iz r-gg6oyi r-ubezar r-16dba41 r-135wba7 r-1m04atk r-1pyaxff" contenteditable="false" style="height:24px">1.</span>
    <span key="6b3418ed58a842968c664d9901398bdd">**Security**<span offset-key="6b3418ed58a842968c664d9901398bdd:1"> - Scope adds security to our code by ensuring that variables can</span></span>

    <span key="1d655b10e8054f63af93514e4c183889"><span offset-key="1d655b10e8054f63af93514e4c183889:0">only be accessed by pre-defined parts of our programs.</span></span>

2.  <span class="r-1awozwy r-1nf4jbm r-6koalj r-18u37iz r-gg6oyi r-ubezar r-16dba41 r-135wba7 r-1m04atk r-1pyaxff" contenteditable="false" style="height:24px">2.</span>
    <span key="fb086c9a81ab453ca6a8dced61e32951">**Reduced Variable Name Collisions**<span offset-key="fb086c9a81ab453ca6a8dced61e32951:1"> - Scope reduces variable name</span></span>

    <span key="5c6c3028a6d846b7937cea466922fa68"><span offset-key="5c6c3028a6d846b7937cea466922fa68:0">collisions, also known as namespace collisions, by ensuring you can use the</span></span>

    <span key="310d3eed69f149d5a1728dab506d8784"><span offset-key="310d3eed69f149d5a1728dab506d8784:0">same variable name multiple times in different scopes without accidentally</span></span>

    <span key="c1ed89fc9a384536b07a93c5ab196c87"><span offset-key="c1ed89fc9a384536b07a93c5ab196c87:0">overwriting those variable's values.</span></span>

## 

<span key="657450e0302045aa9ab494aa19d8dd13"><span offset-key="657450e0302045aa9ab494aa19d8dd13:0">Different kinds of scope</span></span>

<span key="fc9708c172b148f788801d8694dedf06"><span offset-key="fc9708c172b148f788801d8694dedf06:0">There are three types of scope in JavaScript: </span>`global scope`<span offset-key="fc9708c172b148f788801d8694dedf06:2">, </span>`local scope`<span offset-key="fc9708c172b148f788801d8694dedf06:4">, and </span>`block scope`<span offset-key="fc9708c172b148f788801d8694dedf06:6">.</span></span>

### 

<span key="9046c0a34b7449dfbe1aa0097c9b28aa"><span offset-key="9046c0a34b7449dfbe1aa0097c9b28aa:0">Global scope</span></span>

<span key="6e53da3cc5554187a20e02e6bb43ed24"><span offset-key="6e53da3cc5554187a20e02e6bb43ed24:0">Let's start by talking about the widest scope there is: </span>*global scope*<span offset-key="6e53da3cc5554187a20e02e6bb43ed24:2">. The </span>*global scope*<span offset-key="6e53da3cc5554187a20e02e6bb43ed24:4"> is represented by the </span>`window`<span offset-key="6e53da3cc5554187a20e02e6bb43ed24:6"> object in the browser and the </span>`global`<span offset-key="6e53da3cc5554187a20e02e6bb43ed24:8"> object in Node.js. Adding attributes to these objects makes them available throughout the entire program. We can show this with a quick example:</span></span>

1

<span key="f6e06906f7ad48f788e6710d1a5be87e"><span class="r-y7gyvo" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="f6e06906f7ad48f788e6710d1a5be87e:0">let</span><span offset-key="f6e06906f7ad48f788e6710d1a5be87e:1"> myName </span><span class="r-11faab8" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="f6e06906f7ad48f788e6710d1a5be87e:2">=</span><span offset-key="f6e06906f7ad48f788e6710d1a5be87e:3"> </span><span class="r-qtrn9a" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="f6e06906f7ad48f788e6710d1a5be87e:4">"Apples"</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="f6e06906f7ad48f788e6710d1a5be87e:5">;</span></span>

2

<span key="701dc9841a4a483eb6389fe8009aba17"><span offset-key="701dc9841a4a483eb6389fe8009aba17:0"><span slate-zero-width="n">​</span></span></span>

3

<span key="92e91e5fe5e244beaa6e30748100f018"><span offset-key="92e91e5fe5e244beaa6e30748100f018:0">console</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="92e91e5fe5e244beaa6e30748100f018:1">.</span><span slate-leaf="true" offset-key="92e91e5fe5e244beaa6e30748100f018:2">log</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="92e91e5fe5e244beaa6e30748100f018:3">(</span><span offset-key="92e91e5fe5e244beaa6e30748100f018:4">myName</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="92e91e5fe5e244beaa6e30748100f018:5">);</span></span>

4

<span key="cdceb710992f4262a0ad77a1dd64c986"><span class="r-17y197c" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="cdceb710992f4262a0ad77a1dd64c986:0">// this myName references the myName variable from this scope,</span></span>

5

<span key="13d014cb470f4a71869134284bd32b3c"><span class="r-17y197c" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="13d014cb470f4a71869134284bd32b3c:0">// so myName will evaluate to "Apples"</span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3NC05MTMyOF8iIGNsYXNzPSJyLWg3Z2RvYiByLTEwcHR1bjciIHN0eWxlPSJ2ZXJ0aWNhbC1hbGlnbjptaWRkbGU7d2lkdGg6MTZweCI+PHBhdGggZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBjbGlwLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGQ9Ik0wIC41QS41LjUgMCAwMS41IDBoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNVY0aC0xVjFIMXY5aDN2MUguNWEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUtLjVWLjV6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTUgNS41YS41LjUgMCAwMS41LS41aDEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS41LjV2MTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LjVoLTEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNXYtMTB6TTYgNnY5aDlWNkg2eiIgZmlsbD0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7" />

Copied!

<span key="4ec0b208b6ed4a898225bf63f41fbe30"><span offset-key="4ec0b208b6ed4a898225bf63f41fbe30:0">The variable </span>`myName`<span offset-key="4ec0b208b6ed4a898225bf63f41fbe30:2"> above is not inside a function, it is just lying out in the open in our code. The </span>`myName`<span offset-key="4ec0b208b6ed4a898225bf63f41fbe30:4"> variable is part of </span>*global scope*<span offset-key="4ec0b208b6ed4a898225bf63f41fbe30:6">. The Global scope is the largest scope that exists, it is the outermost scope that exists.</span></span>

<span key="bad26b20d777402f9547ddbe1473775e"><span offset-key="bad26b20d777402f9547ddbe1473775e:0">While useful on occasion, global variables are best avoided. Every time a variable is declared on the global scope, the chance of a name collision increases. If we are unaware of the global variables in our code, we may accidentally overwrite variables.</span></span>

### 

<span key="cfdfa37e35e6474782ee480b2025498e"><span offset-key="cfdfa37e35e6474782ee480b2025498e:0">Local scope</span></span>

<span key="d3d3f9ccd3104bf4952d2b0fe18de57b"><span offset-key="d3d3f9ccd3104bf4952d2b0fe18de57b:0">The </span>**scope**<span offset-key="d3d3f9ccd3104bf4952d2b0fe18de57b:2"> of a function is the set of variables that are available for use within that function. We call the scope within a function: </span>*local scope*<span offset-key="d3d3f9ccd3104bf4952d2b0fe18de57b:4">. The </span>*local scope*<span offset-key="d3d3f9ccd3104bf4952d2b0fe18de57b:6"> of a function includes:</span></span>

1.  <span class="r-1awozwy r-1nf4jbm r-6koalj r-18u37iz r-gg6oyi r-ubezar r-16dba41 r-135wba7 r-1m04atk r-1pyaxff" contenteditable="false" style="height:24px">1.</span>
    <span key="befeeeb9b3c24928aac7a089af9660d0"><span offset-key="befeeeb9b3c24928aac7a089af9660d0:0">the function's arguments</span></span>

2.  <span class="r-1awozwy r-1nf4jbm r-6koalj r-18u37iz r-gg6oyi r-ubezar r-16dba41 r-135wba7 r-1m04atk r-1pyaxff" contenteditable="false" style="height:24px">2.</span>
    <span key="3a444b9ba82441348ff25b24ce82db0b"><span offset-key="3a444b9ba82441348ff25b24ce82db0b:0">any local variables declared inside the function</span></span>

3.  <span class="r-1awozwy r-1nf4jbm r-6koalj r-18u37iz r-gg6oyi r-ubezar r-16dba41 r-135wba7 r-1m04atk r-1pyaxff" contenteditable="false" style="height:24px">3.</span>
    <span key="ffd8244549d1445e9a4f19ad8179d4b7">**any variables that were already declared when the function was defined**</span>

<span key="7e5e9e8b52b5452c879a6dd3e96bfeb0"><span offset-key="7e5e9e8b52b5452c879a6dd3e96bfeb0:0">In JavaScript when we enter a new function we enter a </span>**new scope**<span offset-key="7e5e9e8b52b5452c879a6dd3e96bfeb0:2">:</span></span>

1

<span key="276545b44fcd425ab2079b66a71ef3ab"><span class="r-17y197c" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="276545b44fcd425ab2079b66a71ef3ab:0">// global scope</span></span>

2

<span key="60a1c7169b8b476f9fc1f7f161cdef4c"><span class="r-y7gyvo" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="60a1c7169b8b476f9fc1f7f161cdef4c:0">let</span><span offset-key="60a1c7169b8b476f9fc1f7f161cdef4c:1"> myName </span><span class="r-11faab8" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="60a1c7169b8b476f9fc1f7f161cdef4c:2">=</span><span offset-key="60a1c7169b8b476f9fc1f7f161cdef4c:3"> </span><span class="r-qtrn9a" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="60a1c7169b8b476f9fc1f7f161cdef4c:4">"global"</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="60a1c7169b8b476f9fc1f7f161cdef4c:5">;</span></span>

3

<span key="eb2fc113a1704fcebaf0a08165a19d49"><span offset-key="eb2fc113a1704fcebaf0a08165a19d49:0"><span slate-zero-width="n">​</span></span></span>

4

<span key="65871547bb0e4a94805e04fcd4b61462"><span class="r-y7gyvo" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="65871547bb0e4a94805e04fcd4b61462:0">function</span><span offset-key="65871547bb0e4a94805e04fcd4b61462:1"> </span><span slate-leaf="true" offset-key="65871547bb0e4a94805e04fcd4b61462:2">function1</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="65871547bb0e4a94805e04fcd4b61462:3">()</span><span offset-key="65871547bb0e4a94805e04fcd4b61462:4"> </span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="65871547bb0e4a94805e04fcd4b61462:5">{</span></span>

<span key="1ad5cebce13d4ebd80cd40c5370133fc"><span offset-key="1ad5cebce13d4ebd80cd40c5370133fc:0"> </span><span class="r-y7gyvo" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="1ad5cebce13d4ebd80cd40c5370133fc:1">let</span><span offset-key="1ad5cebce13d4ebd80cd40c5370133fc:2"> myName </span><span class="r-11faab8" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="1ad5cebce13d4ebd80cd40c5370133fc:3">=</span><span offset-key="1ad5cebce13d4ebd80cd40c5370133fc:4"> </span><span class="r-qtrn9a" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="1ad5cebce13d4ebd80cd40c5370133fc:5">"func1"</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="1ad5cebce13d4ebd80cd40c5370133fc:6">;</span></span>

<span key="afebd44fdfad470eb1aef47a104dd95c"><span offset-key="afebd44fdfad470eb1aef47a104dd95c:0">console</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="afebd44fdfad470eb1aef47a104dd95c:1">.</span><span slate-leaf="true" offset-key="afebd44fdfad470eb1aef47a104dd95c:2">log</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="afebd44fdfad470eb1aef47a104dd95c:3">(</span><span class="r-qtrn9a" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="afebd44fdfad470eb1aef47a104dd95c:4">"global myName: "</span><span offset-key="afebd44fdfad470eb1aef47a104dd95c:5"> </span><span class="r-11faab8" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="afebd44fdfad470eb1aef47a104dd95c:6">+</span><span offset-key="afebd44fdfad470eb1aef47a104dd95c:7"> myName</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="afebd44fdfad470eb1aef47a104dd95c:8">);</span><span offset-key="afebd44fdfad470eb1aef47a104dd95c:9"> </span><span class="r-17y197c" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="afebd44fdfad470eb1aef47a104dd95c:10">// global myName: global</span></span>

Copied!

<span key="4faeca37ced443d2bda06c75c5a0fb0d"><span offset-key="4faeca37ced443d2bda06c75c5a0fb0d:0">In the code above we are dealing with three different scopes: the global scope, </span>`function1`<span offset-key="4faeca37ced443d2bda06c75c5a0fb0d:2">, and </span>`function2`<span offset-key="4faeca37ced443d2bda06c75c5a0fb0d:4">. Since each of the </span>`myName`<span offset-key="4faeca37ced443d2bda06c75c5a0fb0d:6"> variables were declared in separate scopes, we </span>*are*<span offset-key="4faeca37ced443d2bda06c75c5a0fb0d:8"> allowed to reuse variable names without any issues. This is because each of the </span>`myName`<span offset-key="4faeca37ced443d2bda06c75c5a0fb0d:10"> variables is bound to their respective functions.</span></span>

### 

<span key="7585e712ff0c4b5eb22a0da43a0dc104"><span offset-key="7585e712ff0c4b5eb22a0da43a0dc104:0">Block scope</span></span>

<span key="e71800646dae4b3f98a798748133a669"><span offset-key="e71800646dae4b3f98a798748133a669:0">A block in JavaScript is denoted by a pair of curly braces (</span>`{}`<span offset-key="e71800646dae4b3f98a798748133a669:2">). Examples of block statements in JavaScript are </span>`if`<span offset-key="e71800646dae4b3f98a798748133a669:4"> conditionals or </span>`for`<span offset-key="e71800646dae4b3f98a798748133a669:6"> and </span>`while`<span offset-key="e71800646dae4b3f98a798748133a669:8"> loops.</span></span>

<span key="77d05e6d60e44204af34fb05f43a7c74"><span offset-key="77d05e6d60e44204af34fb05f43a7c74:0">When using the keywords </span>`let`<span offset-key="77d05e6d60e44204af34fb05f43a7c74:2"> or </span>`const`<span offset-key="77d05e6d60e44204af34fb05f43a7c74:4"> the variables defined within the curly braces will be </span>*block scoped*<span offset-key="77d05e6d60e44204af34fb05f43a7c74:6">. Let's look at an example:</span></span>

1

<span key="12cbdb43629e4572a7b64d0ff500841b"><span class="r-17y197c" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="12cbdb43629e4572a7b64d0ff500841b:0">// global scope</span></span>

2

### 

<span key="d1119cd654174e88ab9d59329ee884eb"><span offset-key="d1119cd654174e88ab9d59329ee884eb:0">Scope chaining: variables and scope</span></span>

<span key="7b2dc3446d294ca59e39aa817ac331ae"><span offset-key="7b2dc3446d294ca59e39aa817ac331ae:0">A key scoping rule in JavaScript is the fact that </span>**an**<span offset-key="7b2dc3446d294ca59e39aa817ac331ae:2"> </span>***inner***<span offset-key="7b2dc3446d294ca59e39aa817ac331ae:4"> </span>**scope does have access to variables in the**<span offset-key="7b2dc3446d294ca59e39aa817ac331ae:6"> </span>***outer***<span offset-key="7b2dc3446d294ca59e39aa817ac331ae:8"> </span>**scope**<span offset-key="7b2dc3446d294ca59e39aa817ac331ae:10">.</span></span>

<span key="94f35cfff36c4e6ca5c078fea96af452"><span offset-key="94f35cfff36c4e6ca5c078fea96af452:0">Let's look at a simple example:</span></span>

1

<span key="7cb1967c4e974cf1bdca4ce880c016cb"><span class="r-y7gyvo" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="7cb1967c4e974cf1bdca4ce880c016cb:0">let</span><span offset-key="7cb1967c4e974cf1bdca4ce880c016cb:1"> name </span><span class="r-11faab8" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="7cb1967c4e974cf1bdca4ce880c016cb:2">=</span><span offset-key="7cb1967c4e974cf1bdca4ce880c016cb:3"> </span><span class="r-qtrn9a" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="7cb1967c4e974cf1bdca4ce880c016cb:4">"Fiona"</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="7cb1967c4e974cf1bdca4ce880c016cb:5">;</span></span>

2

<span key="345f825be78c4f88a68f6461f8cdce9d"><span offset-key="345f825be78c4f88a68f6461f8cdce9d:0"><span slate-zero-width="n">​</span></span></span>

<span key="cefc454c1924424ea35b9eafa2099caa"><span class="r-17y197c" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="cefc454c1924424ea35b9eafa2099caa:0">// we aren't passing in or defining and variables</span></span>

4

<span key="b5f65c6ac3d94efca4c81a01dbe66a08"><span class="r-y7gyvo" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="b5f65c6ac3d94efca4c81a01dbe66a08:0">function</span><span offset-key="b5f65c6ac3d94efca4c81a01dbe66a08:1"> </span><span slate-leaf="true" offset-key="b5f65c6ac3d94efca4c81a01dbe66a08:2">hungryHippo</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="b5f65c6ac3d94efca4c81a01dbe66a08:3">()</span><span offset-key="b5f65c6ac3d94efca4c81a01dbe66a08:4"> </span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="b5f65c6ac3d94efca4c81a01dbe66a08:5">{</span></span>

<span key="017c21ba8dfc452894c1dda85f6d5f34"><span slate-leaf="true" offset-key="017c21ba8dfc452894c1dda85f6d5f34:0">hungryHippo</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="017c21ba8dfc452894c1dda85f6d5f34:1">();</span><span offset-key="017c21ba8dfc452894c1dda85f6d5f34:2"> </span><span class="r-17y197c" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="017c21ba8dfc452894c1dda85f6d5f34:3">// => "Fiona is hungry"</span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3NC05MTMyOF8iIGNsYXNzPSJyLWg3Z2RvYiByLTEwcHR1bjcgci0xdnppOHhpIiBzdHlsZT0id2lkdGg6MTZweCI+PHBhdGggZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBjbGlwLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGQ9Ik0wIC41QS41LjUgMCAwMS41IDBoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNVY0aC0xVjFIMXY5aDN2MUguNWEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUtLjVWLjV6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTUgNS41YS41LjUgMCAwMS41LS41aDEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS41LjV2MTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LjVoLTEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNXYtMTB6TTYgNnY5aDlWNkg2eiIgZmlsbD0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

Copied!

<span key="22847c057d46407f9a0ccaddf3649976"><span offset-key="22847c057d46407f9a0ccaddf3649976:0">So when the </span>`hungryHippo`<span offset-key="22847c057d46407f9a0ccaddf3649976:2"> function is declared a new local scope will be created for that function. Continuing on that line of thought what happens when we refer to </span>`name`<span offset-key="22847c057d46407f9a0ccaddf3649976:4"> inside of </span>`hungryHippo`<span offset-key="22847c057d46407f9a0ccaddf3649976:6">? If the </span>`name`<span offset-key="22847c057d46407f9a0ccaddf3649976:8"> variable is not found in the immediate scope, JavaScript will search all of the accessible outer scopes until it finds a variable name that matches the one we are referencing. Once it finds the first matching variable, it will stop searching. In JavaScript this is called </span>*scope chaining*<span offset-key="22847c057d46407f9a0ccaddf3649976:10">.</span></span>

<span key="b534dd7d848b4bdbb21e773da4aca872"><span offset-key="b534dd7d848b4bdbb21e773da4aca872:0">Now let's look at an example of scope chaining with nested scope. Just like functions in JavaScript, a scope can be nested within another scope. Take a look at the example below:</span></span>

1

<span key="fb026055813d48cd9514d7f52d5924ed"><span class="r-17y197c" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="fb026055813d48cd9514d7f52d5924ed:0">// global scope</span></span>

2

<span key="1cf40d038ea14928b16572dc1830fcdb"><span class="r-y7gyvo" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="1cf40d038ea14928b16572dc1830fcdb:0">let</span><span offset-key="1cf40d038ea14928b16572dc1830fcdb:1"> person </span><span class="r-11faab8" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="1cf40d038ea14928b16572dc1830fcdb:2">=</span><span offset-key="1cf40d038ea14928b16572dc1830fcdb:3"> </span><span class="r-qtrn9a" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="1cf40d038ea14928b16572dc1830fcdb:4">"Rae"</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="1cf40d038ea14928b16572dc1830fcdb:5">;</span></span>

<span key="329be8365cdc4477a0bf69974c72c4d0"><span offset-key="329be8365cdc4477a0bf69974c72c4d0:0"> </span><span class="r-y7gyvo" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="329be8365cdc4477a0bf69974c72c4d0:1">let</span><span offset-key="329be8365cdc4477a0bf69974c72c4d0:2"> person </span><span class="r-11faab8" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="329be8365cdc4477a0bf69974c72c4d0:3">=</span><span offset-key="329be8365cdc4477a0bf69974c72c4d0:4"> </span><span class="r-qtrn9a" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="329be8365cdc4477a0bf69974c72c4d0:5">"Jeff"</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="329be8365cdc4477a0bf69974c72c4d0:6">;</span></span>

<span key="58806cc638f94ec0a3db15421d388eaa"><span offset-key="58806cc638f94ec0a3db15421d388eaa:0"> console</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="58806cc638f94ec0a3db15421d388eaa:1">.</span><span slate-leaf="true" offset-key="58806cc638f94ec0a3db15421d388eaa:2">log</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="58806cc638f94ec0a3db15421d388eaa:3">(</span><span class="r-qtrn9a" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="58806cc638f94ec0a3db15421d388eaa:4">"Hi, "</span><span offset-key="58806cc638f94ec0a3db15421d388eaa:5"> </span><span class="r-11faab8" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="58806cc638f94ec0a3db15421d388eaa:6">+</span><span offset-key="58806cc638f94ec0a3db15421d388eaa:7"> person </span><span class="r-11faab8" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="58806cc638f94ec0a3db15421d388eaa:8">+</span><span offset-key="58806cc638f94ec0a3db15421d388eaa:9"> </span><span class="r-qtrn9a" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="58806cc638f94ec0a3db15421d388eaa:10">"!"</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="58806cc638f94ec0a3db15421d388eaa:11">);</span></span>

<span key="217c196bc5a44a22808073ae41372520"><span slate-leaf="true" offset-key="217c196bc5a44a22808073ae41372520:0">sayHello</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="217c196bc5a44a22808073ae41372520:1">();</span><span offset-key="217c196bc5a44a22808073ae41372520:2"> </span><span class="r-17y197c" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="217c196bc5a44a22808073ae41372520:3">// logs 'Hi, Jeff!'</span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3NC05MTMyOF8iIGNsYXNzPSJyLWg3Z2RvYiByLTEwcHR1bjcgci0xdnppOHhpIiBzdHlsZT0id2lkdGg6MTZweCI+PHBhdGggZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBjbGlwLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGQ9Ik0wIC41QS41LjUgMCAwMS41IDBoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNVY0aC0xVjFIMXY5aDN2MUguNWEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUtLjVWLjV6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTUgNS41YS41LjUgMCAwMS41LS41aDEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS41LjV2MTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LjVoLTEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNXYtMTB6TTYgNnY5aDlWNkg2eiIgZmlsbD0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

Copied!

<span key="52bc9f4a75444da9be4741bd6d17b84f"><span offset-key="52bc9f4a75444da9be4741bd6d17b84f:0">In the example above, the variable </span>`person`<span offset-key="52bc9f4a75444da9be4741bd6d17b84f:2"> is referenced by </span>`greet`<span offset-key="52bc9f4a75444da9be4741bd6d17b84f:4">, even though it was never declared within </span>`greet`<span offset-key="52bc9f4a75444da9be4741bd6d17b84f:6">! When this code is executed JavaScript will attempt to run the </span>`greet`<span offset-key="52bc9f4a75444da9be4741bd6d17b84f:8"> function - notice there is no </span>`person`<span offset-key="52bc9f4a75444da9be4741bd6d17b84f:10"> variable within the scope of the </span>`greet`<span offset-key="52bc9f4a75444da9be4741bd6d17b84f:12"> function and move on to seeing if that variable is defined in an outer scope.</span></span>

<span key="e66d91deb7e142db9843f9f8254fad68"><span offset-key="e66d91deb7e142db9843f9f8254fad68:0">Notice that the </span>`greet`<span offset-key="e66d91deb7e142db9843f9f8254fad68:2"> function prints out </span>`Hi, Jeff!`<span offset-key="e66d91deb7e142db9843f9f8254fad68:4"> instead of </span>`Hi, Rae!`<span offset-key="e66d91deb7e142db9843f9f8254fad68:6">. This is because JavaScript will start at the inner most scope looking for a variable named </span>`person`<span offset-key="e66d91deb7e142db9843f9f8254fad68:8">. Then JavaScript will work it's way outward looking for a variable with a matching name of </span>`person`<span offset-key="e66d91deb7e142db9843f9f8254fad68:10">. Since the </span>`person`<span offset-key="e66d91deb7e142db9843f9f8254fad68:12"> variable within </span>`sayHello`<span offset-key="e66d91deb7e142db9843f9f8254fad68:14"> is in the next level of scope above </span>`greet`<span offset-key="e66d91deb7e142db9843f9f8254fad68:16"> JavaScript then stops it's scope chaining search and assigns the value of the </span>`person`<span offset-key="e66d91deb7e142db9843f9f8254fad68:18"> variable.</span></span>

<span key="a7b26d32bfed425f960ce95720596f9f"><span offset-key="a7b26d32bfed425f960ce95720596f9f:0">Functions such as </span>`greet`<span offset-key="a7b26d32bfed425f960ce95720596f9f:2"> that use (ie. </span>**capture**<span offset-key="a7b26d32bfed425f960ce95720596f9f:4">) variables like the person variable are called </span>**closures**<span offset-key="a7b26d32bfed425f960ce95720596f9f:6">. We'll be talking a lot more about closures very soon!</span></span>

<span key="9946f49bb82c42b286432974b68e62a6">**Important**<span offset-key="9946f49bb82c42b286432974b68e62a6:1"> An inner scope can reference outer variables, but an outer scope cannot reference inner variables:</span></span>

1

2

<span key="7f7dd3405592432e8a13e82bb6467206"><span offset-key="7f7dd3405592432e8a13e82bb6467206:0"> </span><span class="r-y7gyvo" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="7f7dd3405592432e8a13e82bb6467206:1">let</span><span offset-key="7f7dd3405592432e8a13e82bb6467206:2"> name </span><span class="r-11faab8" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="7f7dd3405592432e8a13e82bb6467206:3">=</span><span offset-key="7f7dd3405592432e8a13e82bb6467206:4"> </span><span class="r-qtrn9a" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="7f7dd3405592432e8a13e82bb6467206:5">"potato"</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="7f7dd3405592432e8a13e82bb6467206:6">;</span></span>

### 

<span key="9b9a8d290fae43c190ce0ef44d8ae14f"><span offset-key="9b9a8d290fae43c190ce0ef44d8ae14f:0">Lexical scope</span></span>

<span key="a391b0796c2d4146a4bbed09913bee5d"><span offset-key="a391b0796c2d4146a4bbed09913bee5d:0">There is one last important concept to talk about when we refer to scope - and that is </span>*lexical scope*<span offset-key="a391b0796c2d4146a4bbed09913bee5d:2">. Whenever you run a piece of JavaScript that code is first parsed before it is actually run. This is known as the </span>*lexing time*<span offset-key="a391b0796c2d4146a4bbed09913bee5d:4">. In the </span>*lexing time*<span offset-key="a391b0796c2d4146a4bbed09913bee5d:6"> your parser resolves variable names to their values when functions are nested.</span></span>

<span key="61bca1d223344db2851bc2503afa6fac"><span offset-key="61bca1d223344db2851bc2503afa6fac:0">The main take away is that </span>*lexical scope*<span offset-key="61bca1d223344db2851bc2503afa6fac:2"> is determined at </span>*lexing time*<span offset-key="61bca1d223344db2851bc2503afa6fac:4"> so we can determine the values of variables without having to run any code. JavaScript is a language </span>**without dynamic**<span offset-key="61bca1d223344db2851bc2503afa6fac:6"> scoping. This means that by looking at a piece of code we can determine the values of variables just by looking at the different scopes involved.</span></span>

<span key="557572a7a553457199f6309002d751a3"><span offset-key="557572a7a553457199f6309002d751a3:0">Let's look at a quick example:</span></span>

1

<span key="27d00723dfaf4f24bb6cfe9138678207"><span class="r-y7gyvo" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="27d00723dfaf4f24bb6cfe9138678207:0">function</span><span offset-key="27d00723dfaf4f24bb6cfe9138678207:1"> </span><span slate-leaf="true" offset-key="27d00723dfaf4f24bb6cfe9138678207:2">outer</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="27d00723dfaf4f24bb6cfe9138678207:3">()</span><span offset-key="27d00723dfaf4f24bb6cfe9138678207:4"> </span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="27d00723dfaf4f24bb6cfe9138678207:5">{</span></span>

2

<span key="3b1dff989d7646748ae6c20f3aa68cf4"><span offset-key="3b1dff989d7646748ae6c20f3aa68cf4:0"> </span><span class="r-y7gyvo" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="3b1dff989d7646748ae6c20f3aa68cf4:1">let</span><span offset-key="3b1dff989d7646748ae6c20f3aa68cf4:2"> x </span><span class="r-11faab8" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="3b1dff989d7646748ae6c20f3aa68cf4:3">=</span><span offset-key="3b1dff989d7646748ae6c20f3aa68cf4:4"> </span><span class="r-11faab8" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="3b1dff989d7646748ae6c20f3aa68cf4:5">5</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="3b1dff989d7646748ae6c20f3aa68cf4:6">;</span></span>

3

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3NC05MTMyOF8iIGNsYXNzPSJyLWg3Z2RvYiByLTEwcHR1bjcgci0xdnppOHhpIiBzdHlsZT0id2lkdGg6MTZweCI+PHBhdGggZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBjbGlwLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGQ9Ik0wIC41QS41LjUgMCAwMS41IDBoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNVY0aC0xVjFIMXY5aDN2MUguNWEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUtLjVWLjV6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTUgNS41YS41LjUgMCAwMS41LS41aDEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS41LjV2MTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LjVoLTEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNXYtMTB6TTYgNnY5aDlWNkg2eiIgZmlsbD0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

Copied!

<span key="a5f8a88283654ba18fa2dff0638b7f7a"><span offset-key="a5f8a88283654ba18fa2dff0638b7f7a:0">In the </span>`inner`<span offset-key="a5f8a88283654ba18fa2dff0638b7f7a:2"> function above we don't need to run the </span>`outer`<span offset-key="a5f8a88283654ba18fa2dff0638b7f7a:4"> function to know what the value of </span>`x`<span offset-key="a5f8a88283654ba18fa2dff0638b7f7a:6"> will be because of </span>*lexical scoping*<span offset-key="a5f8a88283654ba18fa2dff0638b7f7a:8">.</span></span>

<span key="f017317e4fde431da71f3f1ee3d6af21"><span offset-key="f017317e4fde431da71f3f1ee3d6af21:0">The </span>**scope**<span offset-key="f017317e4fde431da71f3f1ee3d6af21:2"> of a program in JavaScript is the set of variables that are available for use within the program. Due to </span>*lexical scoping*<span offset-key="f017317e4fde431da71f3f1ee3d6af21:4"> we can determine the value of a variable by looking at various scopes without having to run our code. </span>*Scope Chaining*<span offset-key="f017317e4fde431da71f3f1ee3d6af21:6"> allows code within an </span>*inner*<span offset-key="f017317e4fde431da71f3f1ee3d6af21:8"> scope to access variables declared in an </span>*outer*<span offset-key="f017317e4fde431da71f3f1ee3d6af21:10"> scope.</span></span>

<span key="2e0772b5a1f043a092dcce38f262cf83"><span offset-key="2e0772b5a1f043a092dcce38f262cf83:0">There are three different scopes:</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="a9b6b6db51444de49ba499a94bad8b0c">*global scope*<span offset-key="a9b6b6db51444de49ba499a94bad8b0c:1"> - the global space is JavaScript</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="323c8485bbc9412e9b9430cfd5c5a773">*local scope*<span offset-key="323c8485bbc9412e9b9430cfd5c5a773:1"> - created when a function is defined</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="fc66aea8bb204e8887173cd7f34d2623">*block scope*<span offset-key="fc66aea8bb204e8887173cd7f34d2623:1"> - created by entering a pair of curly braces</span></span>

# 

<span key="0c6cc4e473a44a499ed4ca505b855649"><span offset-key="0c6cc4e473a44a499ed4ca505b855649:0">Different Kinds of Variables</span></span>

<span key="81bed82ae1994252b071c6e3a93bed20">**Variables**<span offset-key="81bed82ae1994252b071c6e3a93bed20:1"> are used to store information to be referenced and manipulated in a computer program. A variable's sole purpose is to label and store data in computer memory. Up to this point we've been using the </span>`let`<span offset-key="81bed82ae1994252b071c6e3a93bed20:3"> keyword as our only way of declaring a JavaScript variable. It's now time to expand your tool set to learn about the different kinds of JavaScript variables you can use!</span></span>

<span key="bbcc3bb68e9940a4b810696b4b0463c4"><span offset-key="bbcc3bb68e9940a4b810696b4b0463c4:0">When you finish this reading, you should be able to:</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="a7d846b5db9742d8a11f56f68484bec4"><span offset-key="a7d846b5db9742d8a11f56f68484bec4:0">Identify the three keywords used to declare a variable in JavaScript</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="c3c5557211df46ba8441a17f9ecb9aff"><span offset-key="c3c5557211df46ba8441a17f9ecb9aff:0">Explain the differences between </span>`const`<span offset-key="c3c5557211df46ba8441a17f9ecb9aff:2">, </span>`let`<span offset-key="c3c5557211df46ba8441a17f9ecb9aff:4"> and </span>`var`</span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="014defcb0551450e9d6f53b79cbfca27"><span offset-key="014defcb0551450e9d6f53b79cbfca27:0">Identify the difference between function and block-scoped variables</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="92733e3694044c9386b309fcf91eb3e0"><span offset-key="92733e3694044c9386b309fcf91eb3e0:0">Paraphrase the concept of hoisting in regards to function and block-scoped</span></span>

    <span key="ea67b7bd649c4e04add295eb09e63055"><span offset-key="ea67b7bd649c4e04add295eb09e63055:0">variables</span></span>

## 

<span key="00c061ca52594589af1a5ecf21e77d0c"><span offset-key="00c061ca52594589af1a5ecf21e77d0c:0">Declaring variables</span></span>

<span key="c9ff00216fcd4cb7a23ef1f271c8c287"><span offset-key="c9ff00216fcd4cb7a23ef1f271c8c287:0">All the code you write in JavaScript is </span>*evaluated*<span offset-key="c9ff00216fcd4cb7a23ef1f271c8c287:2">. </span>**A variable always evaluates to the value it contains no matter how you declare it.**</span>

### 

<span key="5b39183da53b4aeeb2d0ab6753d50c63"><span offset-key="5b39183da53b4aeeb2d0ab6753d50c63:0">The different ways to declare variables</span></span>

<span key="1c3eadcbd90742658e9251e1a4cb1b72"><span offset-key="1c3eadcbd90742658e9251e1a4cb1b72:0">In the beginning there was </span>`var`<span offset-key="1c3eadcbd90742658e9251e1a4cb1b72:2">. The </span>`var`<span offset-key="1c3eadcbd90742658e9251e1a4cb1b72:4"> keyword used to be the only way to declare a JavaScript variable. However, in ECMAScript 2015 JavaScript introduced two new ways of declaring JavaScript variables: </span>`let`<span offset-key="1c3eadcbd90742658e9251e1a4cb1b72:6"> and </span>`const`<span offset-key="1c3eadcbd90742658e9251e1a4cb1b72:8">. Meaning, in JavaScript there are </span>**three different ways to declare a variable**<span offset-key="1c3eadcbd90742658e9251e1a4cb1b72:10">. Each of these keywords has advantages and disadvantages and we will now talk about each keyword at length.</span></span>

1.  <span class="r-1awozwy r-1nf4jbm r-6koalj r-18u37iz r-gg6oyi r-ubezar r-16dba41 r-135wba7 r-1m04atk r-1pyaxff" contenteditable="false" style="height:24px">1.</span>
    <span key="f0404b02681a420d8ac39102222155f7">`let`<span offset-key="f0404b02681a420d8ac39102222155f7:1">: any variables declared with the keyword </span>`let`<span offset-key="f0404b02681a420d8ac39102222155f7:3"> </span>*allows you to reassign*</span>

    <span key="7a4ac08b7a07489dbc8651b644c72275"><span offset-key="7a4ac08b7a07489dbc8651b644c72275:0">that variable. Variable declared using </span>`let`<span offset-key="7a4ac08b7a07489dbc8651b644c72275:2"> is scoped within a </span>**block**<span offset-key="7a4ac08b7a07489dbc8651b644c72275:4">.</span></span>

2.  <span class="r-1awozwy r-1nf4jbm r-6koalj r-18u37iz r-gg6oyi r-ubezar r-16dba41 r-135wba7 r-1m04atk r-1pyaxff" contenteditable="false" style="height:24px">2.</span>
    <span key="69d24fe4f6454dfaa08acef6835481a2">`const`<span offset-key="69d24fe4f6454dfaa08acef6835481a2:1">: any variables declared with the keyword </span>`const`<span offset-key="69d24fe4f6454dfaa08acef6835481a2:3"> \_will not allow you</span></span>

    <span key="3e161423401a449282d58a7d2cc99ac8"><span offset-key="3e161423401a449282d58a7d2cc99ac8:0">to reassign\_ that variable. Variable declared using </span>`const`<span offset-key="3e161423401a449282d58a7d2cc99ac8:2"> is scoped within</span></span>

    <span key="cb700931ab6b431ab781cef17e87b955"><span offset-key="cb700931ab6b431ab781cef17e87b955:0">a </span>**block**<span offset-key="cb700931ab6b431ab781cef17e87b955:2">.</span></span>

3.  <span class="r-1awozwy r-1nf4jbm r-6koalj r-18u37iz r-gg6oyi r-ubezar r-16dba41 r-135wba7 r-1m04atk r-1pyaxff" contenteditable="false" style="height:24px">3.</span>
    <span key="5ca61df11e524bfbb09ae1eaef2e2b33">`var`<span offset-key="5ca61df11e524bfbb09ae1eaef2e2b33:1">: A </span>`var`<span offset-key="5ca61df11e524bfbb09ae1eaef2e2b33:3"> declared variable may or may not be reassigned, and the</span></span>

    <span key="4cc3891d3061425285401f4c3d2d1dc9"><span offset-key="4cc3891d3061425285401f4c3d2d1dc9:0">variable is </span>**scoped to a function**<span offset-key="4cc3891d3061425285401f4c3d2d1dc9:2">.</span></span>

<span key="08fac0ec296e4092a679910153053f16"><span offset-key="08fac0ec296e4092a679910153053f16:0">For this course and for your programming career moving forward we recommend you </span>**always**<span offset-key="08fac0ec296e4092a679910153053f16:2"> use </span>`let`<span offset-key="08fac0ec296e4092a679910153053f16:4"> & </span>`const`<span offset-key="08fac0ec296e4092a679910153053f16:6">. These two words allow us to be the most clear with our intentions for the variable we are creating.</span></span>

## 

<span key="415b0768d907498ea55f1cedebba7ec6"><span offset-key="415b0768d907498ea55f1cedebba7ec6:0">Hoisting and scoping with variables</span></span>

<span key="0a12e909169a4c4087c10ef486206e62"><span offset-key="0a12e909169a4c4087c10ef486206e62:0">A wonderful definition of hoisting by Mabishi Wakio, "Hoisting is a JavaScript mechanism where variables and function declarations are moved to the top of their scope before code execution."</span></span>

<span key="e4308bf18a13486c873463151529fcc9"><span offset-key="e4308bf18a13486c873463151529fcc9:0">What this means is that when you run JavaScript code the variables and function declarations will be </span>*hoisted*<span offset-key="e4308bf18a13486c873463151529fcc9:2"> to the top of their particular scope. This is important because </span>`const`<span offset-key="e4308bf18a13486c873463151529fcc9:4"> and </span>`let`<span offset-key="e4308bf18a13486c873463151529fcc9:6"> are </span>**block-scoped**<span offset-key="e4308bf18a13486c873463151529fcc9:8"> while </span>`var`<span offset-key="e4308bf18a13486c873463151529fcc9:10"> is </span>**function-scoped**<span offset-key="e4308bf18a13486c873463151529fcc9:12">.</span></span>

<span key="8311d594889c48b9bebd905983ca6cd0"><span offset-key="8311d594889c48b9bebd905983ca6cd0:0">Let's start by talking more about all </span>`const`<span offset-key="8311d594889c48b9bebd905983ca6cd0:2">, </span>`let`<span offset-key="8311d594889c48b9bebd905983ca6cd0:4">, and </span>`var`<span offset-key="8311d594889c48b9bebd905983ca6cd0:6"> before we dive into why the difference of scopes and hoisting is important.</span></span>

### 

<span key="b17c215c10234d3a8cc84788238d8c51"><span offset-key="b17c215c10234d3a8cc84788238d8c51:0">Function-scoped variables</span></span>

<span key="7bf208df99ba42c989e02549d2d6d472"><span offset-key="7bf208df99ba42c989e02549d2d6d472:0">When JavaScript was young the only available variable was </span>`var`<span offset-key="7bf208df99ba42c989e02549d2d6d472:2">. The </span>`var`<span offset-key="7bf208df99ba42c989e02549d2d6d472:4"> keyword creates </span>*function-scoped*<span offset-key="7bf208df99ba42c989e02549d2d6d472:6"> variables. That means when you use the </span>`var`<span offset-key="7bf208df99ba42c989e02549d2d6d472:8"> keyword to declare a variable that variable will be confined to the scope of the current function.</span></span>

<span key="b18b9cc402b145e19050e3a18f6aa679"><span offset-key="b18b9cc402b145e19050e3a18f6aa679:0">Here is a simple example of declaring a </span>`var`<span offset-key="b18b9cc402b145e19050e3a18f6aa679:2"> variable within a function:</span></span>

1

<span key="f33b855f876c49cda07272cc9832190c"><span class="r-y7gyvo" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="f33b855f876c49cda07272cc9832190c:0">function</span><span offset-key="f33b855f876c49cda07272cc9832190c:1"> </span><span slate-leaf="true" offset-key="f33b855f876c49cda07272cc9832190c:2">test</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="f33b855f876c49cda07272cc9832190c:3">()</span><span offset-key="f33b855f876c49cda07272cc9832190c:4"> </span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="f33b855f876c49cda07272cc9832190c:5">{</span></span>

2

<span key="a31d728fe1f54471a70b3cdecc8d2879"><span offset-key="a31d728fe1f54471a70b3cdecc8d2879:0"> </span><span class="r-y7gyvo" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="a31d728fe1f54471a70b3cdecc8d2879:1">var</span><span offset-key="a31d728fe1f54471a70b3cdecc8d2879:2"> a </span><span class="r-11faab8" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="a31d728fe1f54471a70b3cdecc8d2879:3">=</span><span offset-key="a31d728fe1f54471a70b3cdecc8d2879:4"> </span><span class="r-11faab8" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="a31d728fe1f54471a70b3cdecc8d2879:5">10</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="a31d728fe1f54471a70b3cdecc8d2879:6">;</span></span>

3

<span key="86942f79bc9341618f76f065c473fad2"><span offset-key="86942f79bc9341618f76f065c473fad2:0"><span slate-zero-width="n">​</span></span></span>

4

<span key="a666ada490304a6ea3dc1483c758570a"><span offset-key="a666ada490304a6ea3dc1483c758570a:0"> console</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="a666ada490304a6ea3dc1483c758570a:1">.</span><span slate-leaf="true" offset-key="a666ada490304a6ea3dc1483c758570a:2">log</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="a666ada490304a6ea3dc1483c758570a:3">(</span><span offset-key="a666ada490304a6ea3dc1483c758570a:4">a</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="a666ada490304a6ea3dc1483c758570a:5">);</span><span offset-key="a666ada490304a6ea3dc1483c758570a:6"> </span><span class="r-17y197c" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="a666ada490304a6ea3dc1483c758570a:7">// => 10</span></span>

5

<span key="9a57ea9f8bbb46f0a6bf2bd12c3d7b5d"><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="9a57ea9f8bbb46f0a6bf2bd12c3d7b5d:0">}</span></span>

<span key="87051ea57c9741d78829b5805a03b68d"><span offset-key="87051ea57c9741d78829b5805a03b68d:0">One of the drawbacks of using </span>`var`<span offset-key="87051ea57c9741d78829b5805a03b68d:2"> is that it is a less indicative way of defining a variable.</span></span>

<span key="f841fce1b3df41ba851438331617be4d">**Hoisting with function-scoped variables**</span>

<span key="0c7306f205864487b007049d375e8562"><span offset-key="0c7306f205864487b007049d375e8562:0">Let's take a look at what hoisting does to a function-scoped variable:</span></span>

1

<span key="c8679e6f3fc04dea969d1ad8568fa253"><span class="r-y7gyvo" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="c8679e6f3fc04dea969d1ad8568fa253:0">function</span><span offset-key="c8679e6f3fc04dea969d1ad8568fa253:1"> </span><span slate-leaf="true" offset-key="c8679e6f3fc04dea969d1ad8568fa253:2">test</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="c8679e6f3fc04dea969d1ad8568fa253:3">()</span><span offset-key="c8679e6f3fc04dea969d1ad8568fa253:4"> </span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="c8679e6f3fc04dea969d1ad8568fa253:5">{</span></span>

2

<span key="764df06c727f4bdc9a33e354620c457e"><span offset-key="764df06c727f4bdc9a33e354620c457e:0"> console</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="764df06c727f4bdc9a33e354620c457e:1">.</span><span slate-leaf="true" offset-key="764df06c727f4bdc9a33e354620c457e:2">log</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="764df06c727f4bdc9a33e354620c457e:3">(</span><span offset-key="764df06c727f4bdc9a33e354620c457e:4">hoistedVar</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="764df06c727f4bdc9a33e354620c457e:5">);</span><span offset-key="764df06c727f4bdc9a33e354620c457e:6"> </span><span class="r-17y197c" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="764df06c727f4bdc9a33e354620c457e:7">// => undefined</span></span>

<span key="a0309c3add4440d9be1cfcb2c0582589"><span offset-key="a0309c3add4440d9be1cfcb2c0582589:0"><span slate-zero-width="n">​</span></span></span>

4

<span key="5ae56d7904384581852e7e04e1534d45"><span offset-key="5ae56d7904384581852e7e04e1534d45:0"> </span><span class="r-y7gyvo" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="5ae56d7904384581852e7e04e1534d45:1">var</span><span offset-key="5ae56d7904384581852e7e04e1534d45:2"> hoistedVar </span><span class="r-11faab8" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="5ae56d7904384581852e7e04e1534d45:3">=</span><span offset-key="5ae56d7904384581852e7e04e1534d45:4"> </span><span class="r-11faab8" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="5ae56d7904384581852e7e04e1534d45:5">10</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="5ae56d7904384581852e7e04e1534d45:6">;</span></span>

<span key="aa659223434446d28f0d3d24d0246dd2"><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="aa659223434446d28f0d3d24d0246dd2:0">}</span></span>

<span key="b4700abc5bdb4b6ebd7da18260d59412"><span offset-key="b4700abc5bdb4b6ebd7da18260d59412:0"><span slate-zero-width="n">​</span></span></span>

<span key="4fa18af0a747492995d90288ddcba7f6"><span slate-leaf="true" offset-key="4fa18af0a747492995d90288ddcba7f6:0">test</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="4fa18af0a747492995d90288ddcba7f6:1">();</span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3NC05MTMyOF8iIGNsYXNzPSJyLWg3Z2RvYiByLTEwcHR1bjcgci0xdnppOHhpIiBzdHlsZT0id2lkdGg6MTZweCI+PHBhdGggZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBjbGlwLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGQ9Ik0wIC41QS41LjUgMCAwMS41IDBoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNVY0aC0xVjFIMXY5aDN2MUguNWEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUtLjVWLjV6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTUgNS41YS41LjUgMCAwMS41LS41aDEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS41LjV2MTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LjVoLTEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNXYtMTB6TTYgNnY5aDlWNkg2eiIgZmlsbD0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

Copied!

<span key="37c09635014049b785d4f0ec16b0577b"><span offset-key="37c09635014049b785d4f0ec16b0577b:0">Huh - that's weird. You'd expect an error from referring to a variable like </span>`hoistedVar`<span offset-key="37c09635014049b785d4f0ec16b0577b:2"> before it's defined, something like: </span>`ReferenceError: hoistedVar is not defined`<span offset-key="37c09635014049b785d4f0ec16b0577b:4">. However this is not the case because of </span>*hoisting*<span offset-key="37c09635014049b785d4f0ec16b0577b:6"> in JavaScript!</span></span>

<span key="a1c28087223f42c8a6f89972c8215479"><span offset-key="a1c28087223f42c8a6f89972c8215479:0">So essentially hoisting will isolate and, in the computer's memory, will declare a variable as the top of it's scope. With a function-scoped variable, </span>`var`<span offset-key="a1c28087223f42c8a6f89972c8215479:2">, the name of the variable will be hoisted to the top of the function. In the above snippet, since </span>`hoistedVar`<span offset-key="a1c28087223f42c8a6f89972c8215479:4"> is declared using the </span>`var`<span offset-key="a1c28087223f42c8a6f89972c8215479:6"> keyword the </span>`hoistedVar`<span offset-key="a1c28087223f42c8a6f89972c8215479:8">'s scope is the </span>`test`<span offset-key="a1c28087223f42c8a6f89972c8215479:10"> function. To be clear what is being hoisted is the </span>*declaration*<span offset-key="a1c28087223f42c8a6f89972c8215479:12">, not the </span>*assignment*<span offset-key="a1c28087223f42c8a6f89972c8215479:14"> itself.</span></span>

<span key="3faa0007290f4de5a28c293cc9546f65"><span offset-key="3faa0007290f4de5a28c293cc9546f65:0">In JavaScript, all variables defined with the </span>`var`<span offset-key="3faa0007290f4de5a28c293cc9546f65:2"> keyword have an initial value of </span>`undefined`<span offset-key="3faa0007290f4de5a28c293cc9546f65:4">. Here is a translation of how JavaScript would deal with hoisting in the above </span>`test`<span offset-key="3faa0007290f4de5a28c293cc9546f65:6"> function:</span></span>

1

<span key="cf6c5a668646450ab0b10e787e0f5b7e"><span class="r-y7gyvo" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="cf6c5a668646450ab0b10e787e0f5b7e:0">function</span><span offset-key="cf6c5a668646450ab0b10e787e0f5b7e:1"> </span><span slate-leaf="true" offset-key="cf6c5a668646450ab0b10e787e0f5b7e:2">test</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="cf6c5a668646450ab0b10e787e0f5b7e:3">()</span><span offset-key="cf6c5a668646450ab0b10e787e0f5b7e:4"> </span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="cf6c5a668646450ab0b10e787e0f5b7e:5">{</span></span>

2

<span key="b635cee7032f4e5aa8a8b120cd5b567e"><span offset-key="b635cee7032f4e5aa8a8b120cd5b567e:0"> </span><span class="r-17y197c" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="b635cee7032f4e5aa8a8b120cd5b567e:1">// JavaScript will declare the variable \*in computer memory\* at the top of it's scope</span></span>

3

<span key="0227186007ad427696cfa2bbd870cff4"><span offset-key="0227186007ad427696cfa2bbd870cff4:0"> </span><span class="r-y7gyvo" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="0227186007ad427696cfa2bbd870cff4:1">var</span><span offset-key="0227186007ad427696cfa2bbd870cff4:2"> hoistedVar</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="0227186007ad427696cfa2bbd870cff4:3">;</span></span>

4

<span key="bd7695b5732f471ca197ea8d2d8a525a"><span offset-key="bd7695b5732f471ca197ea8d2d8a525a:0"><span slate-zero-width="n">​</span></span></span>

5

<span key="063e7478cf754b4cbbab67817e05f8eb"><span offset-key="063e7478cf754b4cbbab67817e05f8eb:0"> </span><span class="r-17y197c" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="063e7478cf754b4cbbab67817e05f8eb:1">// since hoisting declared the variable above we now get</span></span>

6

<span key="610634418cfe49e69a0c09826f6e55de"><span offset-key="610634418cfe49e69a0c09826f6e55de:0"> </span><span class="r-17y197c" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="610634418cfe49e69a0c09826f6e55de:1">// the value of 'undefined'</span></span>

7

<span key="bfc72bfdbee84f77aeff6c6b1499cd6c"><span offset-key="bfc72bfdbee84f77aeff6c6b1499cd6c:0"> console</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="bfc72bfdbee84f77aeff6c6b1499cd6c:1">.</span><span slate-leaf="true" offset-key="bfc72bfdbee84f77aeff6c6b1499cd6c:2">log</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="bfc72bfdbee84f77aeff6c6b1499cd6c:3">(</span><span offset-key="bfc72bfdbee84f77aeff6c6b1499cd6c:4">hoistedVar</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="bfc72bfdbee84f77aeff6c6b1499cd6c:5">);</span><span offset-key="bfc72bfdbee84f77aeff6c6b1499cd6c:6"> </span><span class="r-17y197c" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="bfc72bfdbee84f77aeff6c6b1499cd6c:7">// => undefined</span></span>

<span key="9dd1df752dbb40058dcad0c296750c96"><span offset-key="9dd1df752dbb40058dcad0c296750c96:0"><span slate-zero-width="n">​</span></span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3NC05MTMyOF8iIGNsYXNzPSJyLWg3Z2RvYiByLTEwcHR1bjcgci0xdnppOHhpIiBzdHlsZT0id2lkdGg6MTZweCI+PHBhdGggZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBjbGlwLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGQ9Ik0wIC41QS41LjUgMCAwMS41IDBoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNVY0aC0xVjFIMXY5aDN2MUguNWEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUtLjVWLjV6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTUgNS41YS41LjUgMCAwMS41LS41aDEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS41LjV2MTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LjVoLTEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNXYtMTB6TTYgNnY5aDlWNkg2eiIgZmlsbD0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

### 

<span key="235c4776c1724f86aa9c514087e378ac"><span offset-key="235c4776c1724f86aa9c514087e378ac:0">Block-scoped variables</span></span>

<span key="f17cdc0ecaf944d4bcad32fbdb2c07fe"><span offset-key="f17cdc0ecaf944d4bcad32fbdb2c07fe:0">When you are declaring a variable with the keyword </span>`let`<span offset-key="f17cdc0ecaf944d4bcad32fbdb2c07fe:2"> or </span>`const`<span offset-key="f17cdc0ecaf944d4bcad32fbdb2c07fe:4"> you are declaring a variable that exists within </span>*block scope*<span offset-key="f17cdc0ecaf944d4bcad32fbdb2c07fe:6">. Blocks in JavaScript are denoted by curly braces(</span>`{}`<span offset-key="f17cdc0ecaf944d4bcad32fbdb2c07fe:8">). The following examples create a block scope: </span>`if`<span offset-key="f17cdc0ecaf944d4bcad32fbdb2c07fe:10"> statements, </span>`while`<span offset-key="f17cdc0ecaf944d4bcad32fbdb2c07fe:12"> loops, </span>`switch`<span offset-key="f17cdc0ecaf944d4bcad32fbdb2c07fe:14"> statements, and </span>`for`<span offset-key="f17cdc0ecaf944d4bcad32fbdb2c07fe:16"> loops.</span></span>

<span key="d369c098a1d04f15a846b3a6c975fbf7">**Using the keyword let**</span>

<span key="3a31a474a6c74566a0bbacd0426a75fd"><span offset-key="3a31a474a6c74566a0bbacd0426a75fd:0">We can use </span>`let`<span offset-key="3a31a474a6c74566a0bbacd0426a75fd:2"> to declare </span>**re-assignable block-scoped variables**<span offset-key="3a31a474a6c74566a0bbacd0426a75fd:4">. You are, of course, very familiar with </span>`let`<span offset-key="3a31a474a6c74566a0bbacd0426a75fd:6"> so let's take a look at how </span>`let`<span offset-key="3a31a474a6c74566a0bbacd0426a75fd:8"> works within a block scope:</span></span>

1

<span key="803b471dd2f6415cac5452617be93362"><span class="r-y7gyvo" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="803b471dd2f6415cac5452617be93362:0">function</span><span offset-key="803b471dd2f6415cac5452617be93362:1"> </span><span slate-leaf="true" offset-key="803b471dd2f6415cac5452617be93362:2">blockScope</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="803b471dd2f6415cac5452617be93362:3">()</span><span offset-key="803b471dd2f6415cac5452617be93362:4"> </span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="803b471dd2f6415cac5452617be93362:5">{</span></span>

2

<span key="fc8197a8e7774c4e9a20e77452eeb5af"><span offset-key="fc8197a8e7774c4e9a20e77452eeb5af:0"> </span><span class="r-y7gyvo" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="fc8197a8e7774c4e9a20e77452eeb5af:1">let</span><span offset-key="fc8197a8e7774c4e9a20e77452eeb5af:2"> test </span><span class="r-11faab8" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="fc8197a8e7774c4e9a20e77452eeb5af:3">=</span><span offset-key="fc8197a8e7774c4e9a20e77452eeb5af:4"> </span><span class="r-qtrn9a" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="fc8197a8e7774c4e9a20e77452eeb5af:5">"upper scope"</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="fc8197a8e7774c4e9a20e77452eeb5af:6">;</span></span>

3

<span key="1d1844f75b8a4f3ba35d61f71629b2c2"><span offset-key="1d1844f75b8a4f3ba35d61f71629b2c2:0"> </span><span class="r-y7gyvo" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="1d1844f75b8a4f3ba35d61f71629b2c2:1">if</span><span offset-key="1d1844f75b8a4f3ba35d61f71629b2c2:2"> </span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="1d1844f75b8a4f3ba35d61f71629b2c2:3">(</span><span class="r-11faab8" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="1d1844f75b8a4f3ba35d61f71629b2c2:4">true</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="1d1844f75b8a4f3ba35d61f71629b2c2:5">)</span><span offset-key="1d1844f75b8a4f3ba35d61f71629b2c2:6"> </span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="1d1844f75b8a4f3ba35d61f71629b2c2:7">{</span></span>

4

<span key="c79aec1b2112444c9e74c02bc8ab51be"><span offset-key="c79aec1b2112444c9e74c02bc8ab51be:0"> </span><span class="r-y7gyvo" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="c79aec1b2112444c9e74c02bc8ab51be:1">let</span><span offset-key="c79aec1b2112444c9e74c02bc8ab51be:2"> test </span><span class="r-11faab8" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="c79aec1b2112444c9e74c02bc8ab51be:3">=</span><span offset-key="c79aec1b2112444c9e74c02bc8ab51be:4"> </span><span class="r-qtrn9a" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="c79aec1b2112444c9e74c02bc8ab51be:5">"lower scope"</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="c79aec1b2112444c9e74c02bc8ab51be:6">;</span></span>

5

<span key="58dae0540ca54d729e358e4139a21095"><span offset-key="58dae0540ca54d729e358e4139a21095:0"> console</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="58dae0540ca54d729e358e4139a21095:1">.</span><span slate-leaf="true" offset-key="58dae0540ca54d729e358e4139a21095:2">log</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="58dae0540ca54d729e358e4139a21095:3">(</span><span offset-key="58dae0540ca54d729e358e4139a21095:4">test</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="58dae0540ca54d729e358e4139a21095:5">);</span><span offset-key="58dae0540ca54d729e358e4139a21095:6"> </span><span class="r-17y197c" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="58dae0540ca54d729e358e4139a21095:7">// "lower scope"</span></span>

6

<span key="93d2890dccd14dd682b7b8743a3c45d7"><span offset-key="93d2890dccd14dd682b7b8743a3c45d7:0"> </span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="93d2890dccd14dd682b7b8743a3c45d7:1">}</span></span>

7

<span key="507e6ea591604e669ca650f1da84e177"><span offset-key="507e6ea591604e669ca650f1da84e177:0"> console</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="507e6ea591604e669ca650f1da84e177:1">.</span><span slate-leaf="true" offset-key="507e6ea591604e669ca650f1da84e177:2">log</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="507e6ea591604e669ca650f1da84e177:3">(</span><span offset-key="507e6ea591604e669ca650f1da84e177:4">test</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="507e6ea591604e669ca650f1da84e177:5">);</span><span offset-key="507e6ea591604e669ca650f1da84e177:6"> </span><span class="r-17y197c" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="507e6ea591604e669ca650f1da84e177:7">// "upper scope"</span></span>

<span key="036b4bd3322345489c3ffc2f3f190357"><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="036b4bd3322345489c3ffc2f3f190357:0">}</span></span>

<span key="7ed2830f94394218958220e0e4e6d94a"><span offset-key="7ed2830f94394218958220e0e4e6d94a:0">In the example above we can see that the </span>`test`<span offset-key="7ed2830f94394218958220e0e4e6d94a:2"> variable was declared twice using the keyword </span>`let`<span offset-key="7ed2830f94394218958220e0e4e6d94a:4"> but since they were declared within different scopes they have different values.</span></span>

<span key="25511667e34a4808955b4d0472ba5a43"><span offset-key="25511667e34a4808955b4d0472ba5a43:0">JavaScript will raise a </span>`SyntaxError`<span offset-key="25511667e34a4808955b4d0472ba5a43:2"> if you try to declare the same </span>`let`<span offset-key="25511667e34a4808955b4d0472ba5a43:4"> variable twice in one block.</span></span>

Copied!

<span key="3e81c9f832934c1681138f23c4d7722f"><span offset-key="3e81c9f832934c1681138f23c4d7722f:0">We can see above that </span>`var`<span offset-key="3e81c9f832934c1681138f23c4d7722f:2"> will allow you to redeclare a variable twice which can lead to some very confusing and frustrating debugging.</span></span>

<span key="25586e7098234724bc8f9aa78dc73f64"><span offset-key="25586e7098234724bc8f9aa78dc73f64:0">Feel free to peruse the </span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Statements/let" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="108e38ce39414d628dc6c86a0a215bb7" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-91324_259-91325-237__"><span data-key="63cbeefa3dff4d3da6bef8a2b959291e"><span data-offset-key="63cbeefa3dff4d3da6bef8a2b959291e:0">documentation</span></span></span></a><span key="016cd0bb7f874277b35ee6d94890a7ff"><span offset-key="016cd0bb7f874277b35ee6d94890a7ff:0"> for the keyword </span>`let`<span offset-key="016cd0bb7f874277b35ee6d94890a7ff:2"> for more examples.</span></span>

<span key="ab6ab002bf7647e5b79c66c0c8bab99f">**Using the keyword const**</span>

<span key="aebd02e13227403080feab0823ffce36"><span offset-key="aebd02e13227403080feab0823ffce36:0">We use </span>`const`<span offset-key="aebd02e13227403080feab0823ffce36:2"> to declare </span>**block-scoped variables**<span offset-key="aebd02e13227403080feab0823ffce36:4"> that can </span>**not**<span offset-key="aebd02e13227403080feab0823ffce36:6"> be reassigned. In JavaScript variables that cannot be reassigned are called </span>**constants**<span offset-key="aebd02e13227403080feab0823ffce36:8">. Constants should be used for values that will not be re-declared or re-assigned.</span></span>

<span key="5f72a819ac044bde8141d1cf8cb9ed36"><span offset-key="5f72a819ac044bde8141d1cf8cb9ed36:0">Properties of constants:</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="f1944c99688847068e403603d8090336"><span offset-key="f1944c99688847068e403603d8090336:0">They are block-scoped like </span>`let`<span offset-key="f1944c99688847068e403603d8090336:2">.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="087110abffa845fa9e055299a55affb8"><span offset-key="087110abffa845fa9e055299a55affb8:0">JavaScript enforces constants by raising an error if you try to reassign them.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="3305d964bf9c4fe7964c96630b7bb4c0"><span offset-key="3305d964bf9c4fe7964c96630b7bb4c0:0">Trying to redeclare a constant with a </span>`var`<span offset-key="3305d964bf9c4fe7964c96630b7bb4c0:2"> or </span>`let`<span offset-key="3305d964bf9c4fe7964c96630b7bb4c0:4"> by the same name will</span></span>

    <span key="f9d988dcc77e4c8896565d0c196b967b"><span offset-key="f9d988dcc77e4c8896565d0c196b967b:0">also raise an error.</span></span>

<span key="8cd6513e41ba45579da48cbd281d1220"><span offset-key="8cd6513e41ba45579da48cbd281d1220:0">Let's look at a quick example of what happens when trying to reassign a constant:</span></span>

1

<span key="c2f444ea4a7847c2a0f2e33f6acee5bb"><span class="r-11faab8" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="c2f444ea4a7847c2a0f2e33f6acee5bb:0">&gt;</span><span offset-key="c2f444ea4a7847c2a0f2e33f6acee5bb:1"> </span><span class="r-y7gyvo" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="c2f444ea4a7847c2a0f2e33f6acee5bb:2">const</span><span offset-key="c2f444ea4a7847c2a0f2e33f6acee5bb:3"> favFood </span><span class="r-11faab8" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="c2f444ea4a7847c2a0f2e33f6acee5bb:4">=</span><span offset-key="c2f444ea4a7847c2a0f2e33f6acee5bb:5"> </span><span class="r-qtrn9a" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="c2f444ea4a7847c2a0f2e33f6acee5bb:6">"cheeseboard pizza"</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="c2f444ea4a7847c2a0f2e33f6acee5bb:7">;</span><span offset-key="c2f444ea4a7847c2a0f2e33f6acee5bb:8"> </span><span class="r-17y197c" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="c2f444ea4a7847c2a0f2e33f6acee5bb:9">// Initializes a constant</span></span>

2

<span key="74559ded088e482d8fede708b109f313"><span class="r-y7gyvo" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="74559ded088e482d8fede708b109f313:0">undefined</span></span>

<span key="acdfa831c2764f67bc745395d55ddd81"><span class="r-11faab8" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="acdfa831c2764f67bc745395d55ddd81:0">&gt;</span><span offset-key="acdfa831c2764f67bc745395d55ddd81:1"> </span><span class="r-y7gyvo" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="acdfa831c2764f67bc745395d55ddd81:2">const</span><span offset-key="acdfa831c2764f67bc745395d55ddd81:3"> favFood </span><span class="r-11faab8" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="acdfa831c2764f67bc745395d55ddd81:4">=</span><span offset-key="acdfa831c2764f67bc745395d55ddd81:5"> </span><span class="r-qtrn9a" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="acdfa831c2764f67bc745395d55ddd81:6">"inferior food"</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="acdfa831c2764f67bc745395d55ddd81:7">;</span><span offset-key="acdfa831c2764f67bc745395d55ddd81:8"> </span><span class="r-17y197c" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="acdfa831c2764f67bc745395d55ddd81:9">// Re-initialization raises an error</span></span>

<span key="951c9fb0241c450eacff524ccce4c15c"><span offset-key="951c9fb0241c450eacff524ccce4c15c:0">TypeError</span><span class="r-11faab8" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="951c9fb0241c450eacff524ccce4c15c:1">:</span><span offset-key="951c9fb0241c450eacff524ccce4c15c:2"> Identifier </span><span class="r-qtrn9a" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="951c9fb0241c450eacff524ccce4c15c:3">'favFood'</span><span offset-key="951c9fb0241c450eacff524ccce4c15c:4"> has already been declared</span></span>

<span key="fef63b212aee4c6184a2f1e3ffcb5b69"><span offset-key="fef63b212aee4c6184a2f1e3ffcb5b69:0">Constants cannot be reassigned but, just like with </span>`let`<span offset-key="fef63b212aee4c6184a2f1e3ffcb5b69:2">, new constants of the same names can be declared within nested scopes.</span></span>

<span key="9c85a47fe4e74d1386d5c308760ba97f"><span offset-key="9c85a47fe4e74d1386d5c308760ba97f:0"> </span><span class="r-y7gyvo" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="9c85a47fe4e74d1386d5c308760ba97f:1">const</span><span offset-key="9c85a47fe4e74d1386d5c308760ba97f:2"> test </span><span class="r-11faab8" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="9c85a47fe4e74d1386d5c308760ba97f:3">=</span><span offset-key="9c85a47fe4e74d1386d5c308760ba97f:4"> </span><span class="r-qtrn9a" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="9c85a47fe4e74d1386d5c308760ba97f:5">"this works!"</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="9c85a47fe4e74d1386d5c308760ba97f:6">;</span></span>
