<span key="174aa7cfece24905b6083196c12c0969"><span offset-key="174aa7cfece24905b6083196c12c0969:0"> </span><span class="r-y7gyvo" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="174aa7cfece24905b6083196c12c0969:1">const</span><span offset-key="174aa7cfece24905b6083196c12c0969:2"> test </span><span class="r-11faab8" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="174aa7cfece24905b6083196c12c0969:3">=</span><span offset-key="174aa7cfece24905b6083196c12c0969:4"> </span><span class="r-qtrn9a" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="174aa7cfece24905b6083196c12c0969:5">"nope!"</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="174aa7cfece24905b6083196c12c0969:6">;</span><span offset-key="174aa7cfece24905b6083196c12c0969:7"> </span><span class="r-17y197c" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="174aa7cfece24905b6083196c12c0969:8">// SyntaxError: Identifier 'test' has already been declared</span></span>

4

<span key="10b3f06018944da5bf31eccea9171520"><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="10b3f06018944da5bf31eccea9171520:0">}</span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3NC05MTMyOF8iIGNsYXNzPSJyLWg3Z2RvYiByLTEwcHR1bjcgci0xdnppOHhpIiBzdHlsZT0id2lkdGg6MTZweCI+PHBhdGggZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBjbGlwLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGQ9Ik0wIC41QS41LjUgMCAwMS41IDBoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNVY0aC0xVjFIMXY5aDN2MUguNWEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUtLjVWLjV6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTUgNS41YS41LjUgMCAwMS41LS41aDEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS41LjV2MTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LjVoLTEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNXYtMTB6TTYgNnY5aDlWNkg2eiIgZmlsbD0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

Copied!

<span key="47e134acd62540ac964fa18dcb2df21b">**Hoisting with block-scoped variables**</span>

<span key="5b9d42fb7f2741c6bf062e11ede4cae8"><span offset-key="5b9d42fb7f2741c6bf062e11ede4cae8:0">When JavaScript ES6 introduced new ways of declaring a variable using </span>`let`<span offset-key="5b9d42fb7f2741c6bf062e11ede4cae8:2"> and </span>`const`<span offset-key="5b9d42fb7f2741c6bf062e11ede4cae8:4"> the idea of block-level hoisting was also introduced. Block scope hoisting allows developers to avoid previous debugging debacles that naturally happened from using </span>`var`<span offset-key="5b9d42fb7f2741c6bf062e11ede4cae8:6">.</span></span>

<span key="00e955ce10db45098c338205ab59bcae"><span offset-key="00e955ce10db45098c338205ab59bcae:0">Let's take a look at what hoisting does to a </span>*block-scoped*<span offset-key="00e955ce10db45098c338205ab59bcae:2"> variable:</span></span>

1

<span key="e524c2dadab24f969177f3b1f4c78534"><span class="r-y7gyvo" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="e524c2dadab24f969177f3b1f4c78534:0">if</span><span offset-key="e524c2dadab24f969177f3b1f4c78534:1"> </span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="e524c2dadab24f969177f3b1f4c78534:2">(</span><span class="r-11faab8" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="e524c2dadab24f969177f3b1f4c78534:3">true</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="e524c2dadab24f969177f3b1f4c78534:4">)</span><span offset-key="e524c2dadab24f969177f3b1f4c78534:5"> </span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="e524c2dadab24f969177f3b1f4c78534:6">{</span></span>

2

<span key="c72328186ca64901b3f2ba98aab09bae"><span offset-key="c72328186ca64901b3f2ba98aab09bae:0"> console</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="c72328186ca64901b3f2ba98aab09bae:1">.</span><span slate-leaf="true" offset-key="c72328186ca64901b3f2ba98aab09bae:2">log</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="c72328186ca64901b3f2ba98aab09bae:3">(</span><span offset-key="c72328186ca64901b3f2ba98aab09bae:4">str</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="c72328186ca64901b3f2ba98aab09bae:5">);</span><span offset-key="c72328186ca64901b3f2ba98aab09bae:6"> </span><span class="r-17y197c" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="c72328186ca64901b3f2ba98aab09bae:7">// => Uncaught ReferenceError: Cannot access 'str' before initialization</span></span>

3

<span key="8832809c18de4de2b774d0c934d54f50"><span offset-key="8832809c18de4de2b774d0c934d54f50:0"> </span><span class="r-y7gyvo" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="8832809c18de4de2b774d0c934d54f50:1">const</span><span offset-key="8832809c18de4de2b774d0c934d54f50:2"> str </span><span class="r-11faab8" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="8832809c18de4de2b774d0c934d54f50:3">=</span><span offset-key="8832809c18de4de2b774d0c934d54f50:4"> </span><span class="r-qtrn9a" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="8832809c18de4de2b774d0c934d54f50:5">"apple"</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="8832809c18de4de2b774d0c934d54f50:6">;</span></span>

4

<span key="309b76a56b934e9aaa9f394c432022dc"><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="309b76a56b934e9aaa9f394c432022dc:0">}</span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3NC05MTMyOF8iIGNsYXNzPSJyLWg3Z2RvYiByLTEwcHR1bjcgci0xdnppOHhpIiBzdHlsZT0id2lkdGg6MTZweCI+PHBhdGggZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBjbGlwLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGQ9Ik0wIC41QS41LjUgMCAwMS41IDBoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNVY0aC0xVjFIMXY5aDN2MUguNWEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUtLjVWLjV6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTUgNS41YS41LjUgMCAwMS41LS41aDEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS41LjV2MTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LjVoLTEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNXYtMTB6TTYgNnY5aDlWNkg2eiIgZmlsbD0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

Copied!

<span key="72560b76ede5446690ae9c614d26b8a3"><span offset-key="72560b76ede5446690ae9c614d26b8a3:0">Looking at the above we can see that an explicit error is thrown if you attempt to use a block-scoped variable before it was declared. This is the typical behavior in a lot of programming languages - that a variable cannot be referred to until initialized to a value.</span></span>

<span key="b81b70031c1340c2bdbaf0fe29e78bd7"><span offset-key="b81b70031c1340c2bdbaf0fe29e78bd7:0">However, JavaScript is still performing hoisting with block-scoped declared variables. The difference lies is how it </span>*initializes*<span offset-key="b81b70031c1340c2bdbaf0fe29e78bd7:2"> them. Meaning that </span>`let`<span offset-key="b81b70031c1340c2bdbaf0fe29e78bd7:4"> and </span>`const`<span offset-key="b81b70031c1340c2bdbaf0fe29e78bd7:6"> variables are </span>**not**<span offset-key="b81b70031c1340c2bdbaf0fe29e78bd7:8"> initialized to the value of </span>`undefined`<span offset-key="b81b70031c1340c2bdbaf0fe29e78bd7:10">.</span></span>

<span key="a2c8c55106b440fd9772c7b2e160e232"><span offset-key="a2c8c55106b440fd9772c7b2e160e232:0">The time before a </span>`let`<span offset-key="a2c8c55106b440fd9772c7b2e160e232:2"> or </span>`const`<span offset-key="a2c8c55106b440fd9772c7b2e160e232:4"> variable is declared, but not used is called the </span>*Temporal Dead Zone*<span offset-key="a2c8c55106b440fd9772c7b2e160e232:6">. A very cool name for a simple idea. Variables declared using </span>`let`<span offset-key="a2c8c55106b440fd9772c7b2e160e232:8"> and </span>`const`<span offset-key="a2c8c55106b440fd9772c7b2e160e232:10"> are not initialized until their definitions are evaluated. Meaning, you will get an error if you try to reference a </span>`let`<span offset-key="a2c8c55106b440fd9772c7b2e160e232:12"> or </span>`const`<span offset-key="a2c8c55106b440fd9772c7b2e160e232:14"> declared variable before it is evaluated.</span></span>

<span key="926775206ae64c39ae9f6a92aa4c2f1c"><span offset-key="926775206ae64c39ae9f6a92aa4c2f1c:0">Let's look at one more example that should illuminate the presence of the </span>*Temporal Dead Zone*<span offset-key="926775206ae64c39ae9f6a92aa4c2f1c:2">:</span></span>

1

<span key="5ba73083016743769166631aca70e6b5"><span class="r-y7gyvo" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="5ba73083016743769166631aca70e6b5:0">var</span><span offset-key="5ba73083016743769166631aca70e6b5:1"> str </span><span class="r-11faab8" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="5ba73083016743769166631aca70e6b5:2">=</span><span offset-key="5ba73083016743769166631aca70e6b5:3"> </span><span class="r-qtrn9a" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="5ba73083016743769166631aca70e6b5:4">"not apple"</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="5ba73083016743769166631aca70e6b5:5">;</span></span>

2

<span key="3c83d43021ec4bcb8a5a14ee8ae59164"><span offset-key="3c83d43021ec4bcb8a5a14ee8ae59164:0"><span slate-zero-width="n">​</span></span></span>

3

<span key="e55a2b8501eb4d358c705769aa80e51d"><span class="r-y7gyvo" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="e55a2b8501eb4d358c705769aa80e51d:0">if</span><span offset-key="e55a2b8501eb4d358c705769aa80e51d:1"> </span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="e55a2b8501eb4d358c705769aa80e51d:2">(</span><span class="r-11faab8" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="e55a2b8501eb4d358c705769aa80e51d:3">true</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="e55a2b8501eb4d358c705769aa80e51d:4">)</span><span offset-key="e55a2b8501eb4d358c705769aa80e51d:5"> </span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="e55a2b8501eb4d358c705769aa80e51d:6">{</span></span>

4

<span key="d658e7bc309a4bb1bbc7a52d524080da"><span offset-key="d658e7bc309a4bb1bbc7a52d524080da:0"> console</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="d658e7bc309a4bb1bbc7a52d524080da:1">.</span><span slate-leaf="true" offset-key="d658e7bc309a4bb1bbc7a52d524080da:2">log</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="d658e7bc309a4bb1bbc7a52d524080da:3">(</span><span offset-key="d658e7bc309a4bb1bbc7a52d524080da:4">str</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="d658e7bc309a4bb1bbc7a52d524080da:5">);</span><span offset-key="d658e7bc309a4bb1bbc7a52d524080da:6"> </span><span class="r-17y197c" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="d658e7bc309a4bb1bbc7a52d524080da:7">//Uncaught ReferenceError: Cannot access 'str' before initialization</span></span>

5

<span key="b141039d802b4b7890cd0e2fdac2ae70"><span offset-key="b141039d802b4b7890cd0e2fdac2ae70:0"> </span><span class="r-y7gyvo" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="b141039d802b4b7890cd0e2fdac2ae70:1">let</span><span offset-key="b141039d802b4b7890cd0e2fdac2ae70:2"> str </span><span class="r-11faab8" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="b141039d802b4b7890cd0e2fdac2ae70:3">=</span><span offset-key="b141039d802b4b7890cd0e2fdac2ae70:4"> </span><span class="r-qtrn9a" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="b141039d802b4b7890cd0e2fdac2ae70:5">"apple"</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="b141039d802b4b7890cd0e2fdac2ae70:6">;</span></span>

6

<span key="419f701af4374ac387b008db827c1457"><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="419f701af4374ac387b008db827c1457:0">}</span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3NC05MTMyOF8iIGNsYXNzPSJyLWg3Z2RvYiByLTEwcHR1bjcgci0xdnppOHhpIiBzdHlsZT0id2lkdGg6MTZweCI+PHBhdGggZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBjbGlwLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGQ9Ik0wIC41QS41LjUgMCAwMS41IDBoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNVY0aC0xVjFIMXY5aDN2MUguNWEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUtLjVWLjV6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTUgNS41YS41LjUgMCAwMS41LS41aDEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS41LjV2MTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LjVoLTEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNXYtMTB6TTYgNnY5aDlWNkg2eiIgZmlsbD0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

Copied!

<span key="37c90704381b4e678d464345edc9ec0c"><span offset-key="37c90704381b4e678d464345edc9ec0c:0">In the above example we can see that inside the </span>`if`<span offset-key="37c90704381b4e678d464345edc9ec0c:2"> block the </span>`let`<span offset-key="37c90704381b4e678d464345edc9ec0c:4"> declared variable, </span>`str`<span offset-key="37c90704381b4e678d464345edc9ec0c:6">, throws an error. Showing that the error thrown by a </span>`let`<span offset-key="37c90704381b4e678d464345edc9ec0c:8"> variable in the temporal dead zone takes precedence over any scope chaining that would attempt to go to the outer scope to find a value for the </span>`str`<span offset-key="37c90704381b4e678d464345edc9ec0c:10"> variable.</span></span>

### 

<span key="2a948523cf1a4c6a8ea723ad39af4f7c"><span offset-key="2a948523cf1a4c6a8ea723ad39af4f7c:0">Function scope vs. block scope</span></span>

<span key="4c9daa75736d462ea22cde964824e00d"><span offset-key="4c9daa75736d462ea22cde964824e00d:0">Let's now take a deeper look at the comparison of using function vs. block scoped variables.</span></span>

<span key="389fc22b6224456c818f80e149227459"><span offset-key="389fc22b6224456c818f80e149227459:0">Let's start with a simple example:</span></span>

1

<span key="13fd6aca9f6e45409555166bcdeb069b"><span class="r-y7gyvo" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="13fd6aca9f6e45409555166bcdeb069b:0">function</span><span offset-key="13fd6aca9f6e45409555166bcdeb069b:1"> </span><span slate-leaf="true" offset-key="13fd6aca9f6e45409555166bcdeb069b:2">partyMachine</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="13fd6aca9f6e45409555166bcdeb069b:3">()</span><span offset-key="13fd6aca9f6e45409555166bcdeb069b:4"> </span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="13fd6aca9f6e45409555166bcdeb069b:5">{</span></span>

2

<span key="17641972cec94f2a9b5ebc6afb79cfb7"><span offset-key="17641972cec94f2a9b5ebc6afb79cfb7:0"> </span><span class="r-y7gyvo" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="17641972cec94f2a9b5ebc6afb79cfb7:1">var</span><span offset-key="17641972cec94f2a9b5ebc6afb79cfb7:2"> string </span><span class="r-11faab8" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="17641972cec94f2a9b5ebc6afb79cfb7:3">=</span><span offset-key="17641972cec94f2a9b5ebc6afb79cfb7:4"> </span><span class="r-qtrn9a" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="17641972cec94f2a9b5ebc6afb79cfb7:5">"party"</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="17641972cec94f2a9b5ebc6afb79cfb7:6">;</span></span>

3

<span key="e6198c22a0044c94af7ef46554a7d44d"><span offset-key="e6198c22a0044c94af7ef46554a7d44d:0"> console</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="e6198c22a0044c94af7ef46554a7d44d:1">.</span><span slate-leaf="true" offset-key="e6198c22a0044c94af7ef46554a7d44d:2">log</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="e6198c22a0044c94af7ef46554a7d44d:3">(</span><span class="r-qtrn9a" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="e6198c22a0044c94af7ef46554a7d44d:4">"this is a "</span><span offset-key="e6198c22a0044c94af7ef46554a7d44d:5"> </span><span class="r-11faab8" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="e6198c22a0044c94af7ef46554a7d44d:6">+</span><span offset-key="e6198c22a0044c94af7ef46554a7d44d:7"> string</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="e6198c22a0044c94af7ef46554a7d44d:8">);</span></span>

4

<span key="14faea2c01134cf6932e9b4fc706cf31"><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="14faea2c01134cf6932e9b4fc706cf31:0">}</span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3NC05MTMyOF8iIGNsYXNzPSJyLWg3Z2RvYiByLTEwcHR1bjcgci0xdnppOHhpIiBzdHlsZT0id2lkdGg6MTZweCI+PHBhdGggZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBjbGlwLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGQ9Ik0wIC41QS41LjUgMCAwMS41IDBoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNVY0aC0xVjFIMXY5aDN2MUguNWEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUtLjVWLjV6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTUgNS41YS41LjUgMCAwMS41LS41aDEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS41LjV2MTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LjVoLTEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNXYtMTB6TTYgNnY5aDlWNkg2eiIgZmlsbD0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

Copied!

<span key="92f0888bd9c34abd9963942ff392c66b"><span offset-key="92f0888bd9c34abd9963942ff392c66b:0">Looks good so far but let's take that example a step farther and see some of the less fun parts of the </span>`var`<span offset-key="92f0888bd9c34abd9963942ff392c66b:2"> keyword in terms of scope:</span></span>

1

<span key="1eca0b596d6441ca9b01da150458d9a5"><span slate-leaf="true" offset-key="1eca0b596d6441ca9b01da150458d9a5:0">partyMachine</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="1eca0b596d6441ca9b01da150458d9a5:1">();</span><span offset-key="1eca0b596d6441ca9b01da150458d9a5:2"> </span><span class="r-17y197c" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="1eca0b596d6441ca9b01da150458d9a5:3">// => "this is a bummer"</span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3NC05MTMyOF8iIGNsYXNzPSJyLWg3Z2RvYiByLTEwcHR1bjcgci0xdnppOHhpIiBzdHlsZT0id2lkdGg6MTZweCI+PHBhdGggZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBjbGlwLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGQ9Ik0wIC41QS41LjUgMCAwMS41IDBoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNVY0aC0xVjFIMXY5aDN2MUguNWEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUtLjVWLjV6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTUgNS41YS41LjUgMCAwMS41LS41aDEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS41LjV2MTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LjVoLTEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNXYtMTB6TTYgNnY5aDlWNkg2eiIgZmlsbD0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

Copied!

<span key="a14bfad0f0a1402a8997f90fa957b230"><span offset-key="a14bfad0f0a1402a8997f90fa957b230:0">We can see in the above example how the flexibility of </span>`var`<span offset-key="a14bfad0f0a1402a8997f90fa957b230:2"> can ultimately be a bad thing. Since </span>`var`<span offset-key="a14bfad0f0a1402a8997f90fa957b230:4"> is function-scoped </span>*and*<span offset-key="a14bfad0f0a1402a8997f90fa957b230:6"> can be reassigned and re-declared without error it is very easy to overwrite variable values by accident.</span></span>

<span key="16b1331c73264c1e95f97208a272ed07"><span offset-key="16b1331c73264c1e95f97208a272ed07:0">This is the problem that ES6 introduced </span>`let`<span offset-key="16b1331c73264c1e95f97208a272ed07:2"> and </span>`const`<span offset-key="16b1331c73264c1e95f97208a272ed07:4"> to solve. Since </span>`let`<span offset-key="16b1331c73264c1e95f97208a272ed07:6"> and </span>`const`<span offset-key="16b1331c73264c1e95f97208a272ed07:8"> are block-scoped it's a lot easier to avoid accidentally overwriting variable values.</span></span>

<span key="55399bfd82994466815c8ccdf33a4a1d"><span offset-key="55399bfd82994466815c8ccdf33a4a1d:0">Let's take a look at the example function above rewritten using </span>`let`<span offset-key="55399bfd82994466815c8ccdf33a4a1d:2"> and </span>`const`<span offset-key="55399bfd82994466815c8ccdf33a4a1d:4">:</span></span>

1

<span key="aaf75f0ce409418fb041ed95ebc1db04"><span class="r-y7gyvo" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="aaf75f0ce409418fb041ed95ebc1db04:0">function</span><span offset-key="aaf75f0ce409418fb041ed95ebc1db04:1"> </span><span slate-leaf="true" offset-key="aaf75f0ce409418fb041ed95ebc1db04:2">partyMachine</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="aaf75f0ce409418fb041ed95ebc1db04:3">()</span><span offset-key="aaf75f0ce409418fb041ed95ebc1db04:4"> </span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="aaf75f0ce409418fb041ed95ebc1db04:5">{</span></span>

<span key="c5625c95d64445549d7074bd734a0d3d"><span offset-key="c5625c95d64445549d7074bd734a0d3d:0"><span slate-zero-width="n">​</span></span></span>

<span key="24d6754534bf4b29991d811db09a88ae"><span offset-key="24d6754534bf4b29991d811db09a88ae:0"> </span><span class="r-y7gyvo" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="24d6754534bf4b29991d811db09a88ae:1">if</span><span offset-key="24d6754534bf4b29991d811db09a88ae:2"> </span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="24d6754534bf4b29991d811db09a88ae:3">(</span><span class="r-11faab8" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="24d6754534bf4b29991d811db09a88ae:4">true</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="24d6754534bf4b29991d811db09a88ae:5">)</span><span offset-key="24d6754534bf4b29991d811db09a88ae:6"> </span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="24d6754534bf4b29991d811db09a88ae:7">{</span></span>

<span key="7d626bde65694b3a84fc2877167ad1b8"><span offset-key="7d626bde65694b3a84fc2877167ad1b8:0"> </span><span class="r-17y197c" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="7d626bde65694b3a84fc2877167ad1b8:1">// this variable is restricted to the scope of this block</span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3NC05MTMyOF8iIGNsYXNzPSJyLWg3Z2RvYiByLTEwcHR1bjcgci0xdnppOHhpIiBzdHlsZT0id2lkdGg6MTZweCI+PHBhdGggZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBjbGlwLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGQ9Ik0wIC41QS41LjUgMCAwMS41IDBoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNVY0aC0xVjFIMXY5aDN2MUguNWEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUtLjVWLjV6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTUgNS41YS41LjUgMCAwMS41LS41aDEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS41LjV2MTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LjVoLTEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNXYtMTB6TTYgNnY5aDlWNkg2eiIgZmlsbD0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

Copied!

## 

<span key="b9da14908b6e4384a6b9880f8f38f0ca"><span offset-key="b9da14908b6e4384a6b9880f8f38f0ca:0">Global variables</span></span>

<span key="9c1f35305fd84e2093c4204579d18bdd"><span offset-key="9c1f35305fd84e2093c4204579d18bdd:0">If you leave off a declaration when initializing a variable, it will become a global. </span>**Do not do this.**<span offset-key="9c1f35305fd84e2093c4204579d18bdd:2"> We declare variables using the keywords </span>`var`<span offset-key="9c1f35305fd84e2093c4204579d18bdd:4">, </span>`let`<span offset-key="9c1f35305fd84e2093c4204579d18bdd:6">, and </span>`const`<span offset-key="9c1f35305fd84e2093c4204579d18bdd:8"> to ensure that our variables are declared within a proper scope. Any variables declared without these keywords will be declared on the </span>*global scope*<span offset-key="9c1f35305fd84e2093c4204579d18bdd:10">.</span></span>

<span key="a6c08295880a42e98c543adf06acdbd2"><span offset-key="a6c08295880a42e98c543adf06acdbd2:0">JavaScript has a single global scope, which means all of the files from your projects and any libraries you use will </span>**all be sharing the same scope**<span offset-key="a6c08295880a42e98c543adf06acdbd2:2">. Every time a variable is declared on the global scope, the chance of a name collision increases. If we are unaware of the global variables in our code, we may accidentally overwrite variables.</span></span>

<span key="6c3de8e9916a459a885b31bc98d8a487"><span offset-key="6c3de8e9916a459a885b31bc98d8a487:0">Let's look at a quick example showing why this is a bad idea:</span></span>

1

<span key="0ccc5921bd334c1a978d2768ce0a97fe"><span class="r-y7gyvo" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="0ccc5921bd334c1a978d2768ce0a97fe:0">function</span><span offset-key="0ccc5921bd334c1a978d2768ce0a97fe:1"> </span><span slate-leaf="true" offset-key="0ccc5921bd334c1a978d2768ce0a97fe:2">good</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="0ccc5921bd334c1a978d2768ce0a97fe:3">()</span><span offset-key="0ccc5921bd334c1a978d2768ce0a97fe:4"> </span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="0ccc5921bd334c1a978d2768ce0a97fe:5">{</span></span>

2

<span key="97978d03598c456b90bf3e2e0cf1f6b8"><span offset-key="97978d03598c456b90bf3e2e0cf1f6b8:0"> </span><span class="r-y7gyvo" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="97978d03598c456b90bf3e2e0cf1f6b8:1">let</span><span offset-key="97978d03598c456b90bf3e2e0cf1f6b8:2"> x </span><span class="r-11faab8" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="97978d03598c456b90bf3e2e0cf1f6b8:3">=</span><span offset-key="97978d03598c456b90bf3e2e0cf1f6b8:4"> </span><span class="r-11faab8" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="97978d03598c456b90bf3e2e0cf1f6b8:5">5</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="97978d03598c456b90bf3e2e0cf1f6b8:6">;</span></span>

3

<span key="e1b11103c90c4381a71d20746f2b6105"><span offset-key="e1b11103c90c4381a71d20746f2b6105:0"> </span><span class="r-y7gyvo" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="e1b11103c90c4381a71d20746f2b6105:1">let</span><span offset-key="e1b11103c90c4381a71d20746f2b6105:2"> y </span><span class="r-11faab8" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="e1b11103c90c4381a71d20746f2b6105:3">=</span><span offset-key="e1b11103c90c4381a71d20746f2b6105:4"> </span><span class="r-qtrn9a" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="e1b11103c90c4381a71d20746f2b6105:5">"yay"</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="e1b11103c90c4381a71d20746f2b6105:6">;</span></span>

4

<span key="587d171ccbfe4bfbb4b518aa2a9599ad"><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="587d171ccbfe4bfbb4b518aa2a9599ad:0">}</span></span>

5

<span key="3795b3fe83f148138c3b834a50422ca4"><span offset-key="3795b3fe83f148138c3b834a50422ca4:0"><span slate-zero-width="n">​</span></span></span>

6

<span key="cae78745185a4f70bdef5b762cf111f9"><span slate-leaf="true" offset-key="cae78745185a4f70bdef5b762cf111f9:0">why</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="cae78745185a4f70bdef5b762cf111f9:1">();</span></span>

Copied!

<span key="f2b6f19a1f804cef97f0a32dfdc38090"><span offset-key="f2b6f19a1f804cef97f0a32dfdc38090:0">Limiting global variables will help you create code that is much more easily maintainable. Strive to write your functions so that they are self-contained and not reliant on outside variables. This will also be a huge help in allowing us test each function by itself.</span></span>

<span key="ca7ee29bfcbe4a11a693c9399ed0ecbf"><span offset-key="ca7ee29bfcbe4a11a693c9399ed0ecbf:0">One of our jobs as programmers is to write code that can be integrated easily within a team. In order to do that, we need to limit the number of globally declared variables in our code as much as possible, to avoid accidental name collisions.</span></span>

<span key="f1508c6e4ea7498589a08f0c12860ba0"><span offset-key="f1508c6e4ea7498589a08f0c12860ba0:0">Sloppy programmers use global variables, and you are not working so hard in order to be a sloppy programmer!</span></span>

<span key="4449dfc8d38f4074884df48b45931b31"><span offset-key="4449dfc8d38f4074884df48b45931b31:0">dentify the different ways to declare a variable in JavaScript</span></span>

    <span key="45809f6115ee4613b616ae2cd567ed4c"><span offset-key="45809f6115ee4613b616ae2cd567ed4c:0">Explain the differences between </span>`const`<span offset-key="45809f6115ee4613b616ae2cd567ed4c:2">, </span>`let`<span offset-key="45809f6115ee4613b616ae2cd567ed4c:4"> and </span>`var`</span>

    <span key="acc96a1ee7364e0e82622aa22965a068"><span offset-key="acc96a1ee7364e0e82622aa22965a068:0">Paraphrase the concept of hoisting in regards to variables</span></span>

# 

<span key="ce9e3e589130415ea2c6ca656a70313c"><span offset-key="ce9e3e589130415ea2c6ca656a70313c:0">Calculating Closures</span></span>

<span key="82cbb01f4be14ba187ed9d465f83fe1a"><span offset-key="82cbb01f4be14ba187ed9d465f83fe1a:0">What is a </span>*closure*<span offset-key="82cbb01f4be14ba187ed9d465f83fe1a:2">? This question is one of the </span>*most frequent interview questions*<span offset-key="82cbb01f4be14ba187ed9d465f83fe1a:4"> where JavaScript is involved. If you answer this question quickly and knowledgeably you'll look like a great candidate. We know you want to know it all so let's dive right in!</span></span>

<span key="a79f7ea765e043a591fda61106b98e58"><span offset-key="a79f7ea765e043a591fda61106b98e58:0">The official definition of a closure from MDN is, "A closure is the combination of a function and the lexical environment within which that function was declared." The practicality of how a </span>*closure*<span offset-key="a79f7ea765e043a591fda61106b98e58:2"> is used it simple: a </span>*closure*<span offset-key="a79f7ea765e043a591fda61106b98e58:4"> is when an inner function uses, or changes, variables in an outer function. Closures in JavaScript are incredibly important in terms of the creativity, flexibility and security of your code.</span></span>

<span key="eb81419b041b446383fedecf3789858b"><span offset-key="eb81419b041b446383fedecf3789858b:0">When you finish this reading you should be able to implement a closure and explain how that closure effects scope.</span></span>

## 

<span key="d1528ddb66e84326a4222ad886d9c2c1"><span offset-key="d1528ddb66e84326a4222ad886d9c2c1:0">Closures and scope</span></span>

<span key="d3623422e7b049c893ffb74899332e42"><span offset-key="d3623422e7b049c893ffb74899332e42:0">Let's look at an example of a simple closure below:</span></span>

1

2

<span key="0ebc327bd2974bf3a01c2399672427e3"><span offset-key="0ebc327bd2974bf3a01c2399672427e3:0"> </span><span class="r-y7gyvo" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="0ebc327bd2974bf3a01c2399672427e3:1">let</span><span offset-key="0ebc327bd2974bf3a01c2399672427e3:2"> treeString </span><span class="r-11faab8" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="0ebc327bd2974bf3a01c2399672427e3:3">=</span><span offset-key="0ebc327bd2974bf3a01c2399672427e3:4"> </span><span class="r-qtrn9a" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="0ebc327bd2974bf3a01c2399672427e3:5">"You climbed a "</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="0ebc327bd2974bf3a01c2399672427e3:6">;</span></span>

<span key="c5947fc494c840a1af840a7f7a7da1ee"><span offset-key="c5947fc494c840a1af840a7f7a7da1ee:0"><span slate-zero-width="n">​</span></span></span>

4

<span key="82f357ef190449ba97d0e8558a6cbb61"><span offset-key="82f357ef190449ba97d0e8558a6cbb61:0"> </span><span class="r-y7gyvo" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="82f357ef190449ba97d0e8558a6cbb61:1">function</span><span offset-key="82f357ef190449ba97d0e8558a6cbb61:2"> </span><span slate-leaf="true" offset-key="82f357ef190449ba97d0e8558a6cbb61:3">sayClimbTree</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="82f357ef190449ba97d0e8558a6cbb61:4">()</span><span offset-key="82f357ef190449ba97d0e8558a6cbb61:5"> </span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="82f357ef190449ba97d0e8558a6cbb61:6">{</span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3NC05MTMyOF8iIGNsYXNzPSJyLWg3Z2RvYiByLTEwcHR1bjcgci0xdnppOHhpIiBzdHlsZT0id2lkdGg6MTZweCI+PHBhdGggZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBjbGlwLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGQ9Ik0wIC41QS41LjUgMCAwMS41IDBoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNVY0aC0xVjFIMXY5aDN2MUguNWEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUtLjVWLjV6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTUgNS41YS41LjUgMCAwMS41LS41aDEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS41LjV2MTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LjVoLTEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNXYtMTB6TTYgNnY5aDlWNkg2eiIgZmlsbD0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

<span key="0fc7d1a97e06424a8b4827063497cefe"><span offset-key="0fc7d1a97e06424a8b4827063497cefe:0">In the above snippet the </span>`sayClimbTree`<span offset-key="0fc7d1a97e06424a8b4827063497cefe:2"> function captures and uses the </span>`treeString`<span offset-key="0fc7d1a97e06424a8b4827063497cefe:4"> and </span>`treeType`<span offset-key="0fc7d1a97e06424a8b4827063497cefe:6"> variables within its own inner scope.</span></span>

<span key="35698b34d9a44b508e20fc22af5841ee"><span offset-key="35698b34d9a44b508e20fc22af5841ee:0">Let's go over some basic closure rules:</span></span>

1.  <span class="r-1awozwy r-1nf4jbm r-6koalj r-18u37iz r-gg6oyi r-ubezar r-16dba41 r-135wba7 r-1m04atk r-1pyaxff" contenteditable="false" style="height:24px">1.</span>
    <span key="d0e87252e36e4827bbf225280f968b4e"><span offset-key="d0e87252e36e4827bbf225280f968b4e:0">Closures have access to any variables within its own, as well as any outer</span></span>

    <span key="c75664db913c480382ded08f19c47055"><span offset-key="c75664db913c480382ded08f19c47055:0">function's, scope when they are declared. This is where the \_lexical</span></span>

    <span key="1608958f0574494fbf3d61db56c64c05"><span offset-key="1608958f0574494fbf3d61db56c64c05:0">environment </span>*comes in - the \_lexical environment*<span offset-key="1608958f0574494fbf3d61db56c64c05:2"> consists of any variables</span></span>

    <span key="4743121351894dd0984e576fd147ce40"><span offset-key="4743121351894dd0984e576fd147ce40:0">available within the scope in which the closure was declared (which are the</span></span>

    <span key="38b0d1a06f594c72b56b2dec5042812e"><span offset-key="38b0d1a06f594c72b56b2dec5042812e:0">local inner scope, outer function's scope, and global scope).</span></span>

2.  <span class="r-1awozwy r-1nf4jbm r-6koalj r-18u37iz r-gg6oyi r-ubezar r-16dba41 r-135wba7 r-1m04atk r-1pyaxff" contenteditable="false" style="height:24px">2.</span>
    <span key="f2a05619baee498fa0fc532ce7c34e88"><span offset-key="f2a05619baee498fa0fc532ce7c34e88:0">A closure will keep reference to all the variables when it was defined \*\*even</span></span>

    <span key="2622b53cd1424d04958585267071769a"><span offset-key="2622b53cd1424d04958585267071769a:0">if the outer function has returned\*\*.</span></span>

<span key="ef18cc2c658c4a3098a583c8def4136f"><span offset-key="ef18cc2c658c4a3098a583c8def4136f:0">Notice above that even though the above </span>`climbTree`<span offset-key="ef18cc2c658c4a3098a583c8def4136f:2"> had run its </span>`return`<span offset-key="ef18cc2c658c4a3098a583c8def4136f:4"> statement the inner function of </span>`sayClimbTree`<span offset-key="ef18cc2c658c4a3098a583c8def4136f:6"> </span>**still has access**<span offset-key="ef18cc2c658c4a3098a583c8def4136f:8"> to the variables(</span>`treeString`<span offset-key="ef18cc2c658c4a3098a583c8def4136f:10"> and </span>`treeType`<span offset-key="ef18cc2c658c4a3098a583c8def4136f:12">) from the outer scope where it was declared. So, even after an outer function has returned, an inner function will still have access to the outer function’s variables.</span></span>

<span key="284b278ca34749a18d90714ce4433ed4"><span offset-key="284b278ca34749a18d90714ce4433ed4:0">Let's look at another example of a closure:</span></span>

1

<span key="e77b5dcee8b9402dbbe97b208220f024"><span class="r-y7gyvo" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="e77b5dcee8b9402dbbe97b208220f024:0">function</span><span offset-key="e77b5dcee8b9402dbbe97b208220f024:1"> </span><span slate-leaf="true" offset-key="e77b5dcee8b9402dbbe97b208220f024:2">makeAdder</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="e77b5dcee8b9402dbbe97b208220f024:3">(</span><span slate-leaf="true" offset-key="e77b5dcee8b9402dbbe97b208220f024:4">x</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="e77b5dcee8b9402dbbe97b208220f024:5">)</span><span offset-key="e77b5dcee8b9402dbbe97b208220f024:6"> </span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="e77b5dcee8b9402dbbe97b208220f024:7">{</span></span>

2

<span key="fcb7ab6fa6864ff781b1e848793c6267"><span offset-key="fcb7ab6fa6864ff781b1e848793c6267:0"> </span><span class="r-y7gyvo" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="fcb7ab6fa6864ff781b1e848793c6267:1">return</span><span offset-key="fcb7ab6fa6864ff781b1e848793c6267:2"> </span><span class="r-y7gyvo" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="fcb7ab6fa6864ff781b1e848793c6267:3">function</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="fcb7ab6fa6864ff781b1e848793c6267:4">(</span><span slate-leaf="true" offset-key="fcb7ab6fa6864ff781b1e848793c6267:5">y</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="fcb7ab6fa6864ff781b1e848793c6267:6">)</span><span offset-key="fcb7ab6fa6864ff781b1e848793c6267:7"> </span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="fcb7ab6fa6864ff781b1e848793c6267:8">{</span></span>

3

<span key="eea1a7bdc6ce44c88ea4592c1001a07a"><span offset-key="eea1a7bdc6ce44c88ea4592c1001a07a:0"> </span><span class="r-y7gyvo" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="eea1a7bdc6ce44c88ea4592c1001a07a:1">return</span><span offset-key="eea1a7bdc6ce44c88ea4592c1001a07a:2"> x </span><span class="r-11faab8" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="eea1a7bdc6ce44c88ea4592c1001a07a:3">+</span><span offset-key="eea1a7bdc6ce44c88ea4592c1001a07a:4"> y</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="eea1a7bdc6ce44c88ea4592c1001a07a:5">;</span></span>

4

<span key="abeb2cb8db9c47a2a0bccdcade9b5795"><span offset-key="abeb2cb8db9c47a2a0bccdcade9b5795:0"> </span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="abeb2cb8db9c47a2a0bccdcade9b5795:1">};</span></span>

5

<span key="3981472aefac4d7885a6c8ba8467e55f"><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="3981472aefac4d7885a6c8ba8467e55f:0">}</span></span>

<span key="99eacb2dfc064925a7b8d104c3314e64"><span class="r-y7gyvo" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="99eacb2dfc064925a7b8d104c3314e64:0">const</span><span offset-key="99eacb2dfc064925a7b8d104c3314e64:1"> add5 </span><span class="r-11faab8" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="99eacb2dfc064925a7b8d104c3314e64:2">=</span><span offset-key="99eacb2dfc064925a7b8d104c3314e64:3"> </span><span slate-leaf="true" offset-key="99eacb2dfc064925a7b8d104c3314e64:4">makeAdder</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="99eacb2dfc064925a7b8d104c3314e64:5">(</span><span class="r-11faab8" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="99eacb2dfc064925a7b8d104c3314e64:6">5</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="99eacb2dfc064925a7b8d104c3314e64:7">);</span></span>

<span key="72cb9b5dc13a4a71bc676cc29ed8a284"><span offset-key="72cb9b5dc13a4a71bc676cc29ed8a284:0">console</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="72cb9b5dc13a4a71bc676cc29ed8a284:1">.</span><span slate-leaf="true" offset-key="72cb9b5dc13a4a71bc676cc29ed8a284:2">log</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="72cb9b5dc13a4a71bc676cc29ed8a284:3">(</span><span slate-leaf="true" offset-key="72cb9b5dc13a4a71bc676cc29ed8a284:4">add5</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="72cb9b5dc13a4a71bc676cc29ed8a284:5">(</span><span class="r-11faab8" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="72cb9b5dc13a4a71bc676cc29ed8a284:6">2</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="72cb9b5dc13a4a71bc676cc29ed8a284:7">));</span><span offset-key="72cb9b5dc13a4a71bc676cc29ed8a284:8"> </span><span class="r-17y197c" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="72cb9b5dc13a4a71bc676cc29ed8a284:9">// prints 7</span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3NC05MTMyOF8iIGNsYXNzPSJyLWg3Z2RvYiByLTEwcHR1bjcgci0xdnppOHhpIiBzdHlsZT0id2lkdGg6MTZweCI+PHBhdGggZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBjbGlwLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGQ9Ik0wIC41QS41LjUgMCAwMS41IDBoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNVY0aC0xVjFIMXY5aDN2MUguNWEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUtLjVWLjV6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTUgNS41YS41LjUgMCAwMS41LS41aDEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS41LjV2MTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LjVoLTEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNXYtMTB6TTYgNnY5aDlWNkg2eiIgZmlsbD0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

Copied!

<span key="b84744d8087242f7ba7a7057c57921e3"><span offset-key="b84744d8087242f7ba7a7057c57921e3:0">In the above example the function the anonymous function within the </span>`makeAdder`<span offset-key="b84744d8087242f7ba7a7057c57921e3:2"> function </span>**closes over**<span offset-key="b84744d8087242f7ba7a7057c57921e3:4"> the </span>`x`<span offset-key="b84744d8087242f7ba7a7057c57921e3:6"> variable and utilizes it within the inner anonymous function. This allows us to do some pretty cool stuff like creating the </span>`add5`<span offset-key="b84744d8087242f7ba7a7057c57921e3:8"> function above. Closures are your friend ❤️.</span></span>

## 

<span key="f4cab43a4343499cb09199ffc10e5b83"><span offset-key="f4cab43a4343499cb09199ffc10e5b83:0">Applications of closures</span></span>

<span key="1d25fb60dccf42e7bfe3832e9bda8975"><span offset-key="1d25fb60dccf42e7bfe3832e9bda8975:0">Let's take a look at some of the common and practical applications of closures in JavaScript.</span></span>

### 

<span key="0d81030b71154108a6e76810229e4a87"><span offset-key="0d81030b71154108a6e76810229e4a87:0">Private State</span></span>

<span key="31d9ba03e8124f0db4e2094572f69707"><span offset-key="31d9ba03e8124f0db4e2094572f69707:0">Information hiding is incredibly important in the world of software engineering. JavaScript as a language does not have a way of declaring a function as exclusively private, as can be done in other programming languages. We can however, use </span>*closures*<span offset-key="31d9ba03e8124f0db4e2094572f69707:2"> to create private state within a function.</span></span>

<span key="0e67631ed6754e47a67fa7ea4ec893de"><span offset-key="0e67631ed6754e47a67fa7ea4ec893de:0">The following code illustrates how to use </span>*closures*<span offset-key="0e67631ed6754e47a67fa7ea4ec893de:2"> to define functions that can emulate private functions and variables:</span></span>

1

<span key="53acbd08e3644a4c9135c17634296af1"><span class="r-y7gyvo" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="53acbd08e3644a4c9135c17634296af1:0">function</span><span offset-key="53acbd08e3644a4c9135c17634296af1:1"> </span><span slate-leaf="true" offset-key="53acbd08e3644a4c9135c17634296af1:2">createCounter</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="53acbd08e3644a4c9135c17634296af1:3">()</span><span offset-key="53acbd08e3644a4c9135c17634296af1:4"> </span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="53acbd08e3644a4c9135c17634296af1:5">{</span></span>

2

<span key="0079f5257c9d4190975822d9c7b7af75"><span offset-key="0079f5257c9d4190975822d9c7b7af75:0"> </span><span class="r-y7gyvo" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="0079f5257c9d4190975822d9c7b7af75:1">let</span><span offset-key="0079f5257c9d4190975822d9c7b7af75:2"> count </span><span class="r-11faab8" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="0079f5257c9d4190975822d9c7b7af75:3">=</span><span offset-key="0079f5257c9d4190975822d9c7b7af75:4"> </span><span class="r-11faab8" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="0079f5257c9d4190975822d9c7b7af75:5">0</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="0079f5257c9d4190975822d9c7b7af75:6">;</span></span>

3

5

<span key="fd0e54aeec9b4b5895e0d795e06876fc"><span class="r-17y197c" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="fd0e54aeec9b4b5895e0d795e06876fc:0">//we cannot reach the count variable!</span></span>

<span key="80828b1ec58a4584992560e2b47de29d"><span offset-key="80828b1ec58a4584992560e2b47de29d:0">counter</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="80828b1ec58a4584992560e2b47de29d:1">.</span><span offset-key="80828b1ec58a4584992560e2b47de29d:2">count</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="80828b1ec58a4584992560e2b47de29d:3">;</span><span offset-key="80828b1ec58a4584992560e2b47de29d:4"> </span><span class="r-17y197c" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="80828b1ec58a4584992560e2b47de29d:5">// undefined</span></span>

<span key="96968406e45648909e9fd52a76ab08cc"><span class="r-y7gyvo" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="96968406e45648909e9fd52a76ab08cc:0">let</span><span offset-key="96968406e45648909e9fd52a76ab08cc:1"> counter2 </span><span class="r-11faab8" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="96968406e45648909e9fd52a76ab08cc:2">=</span><span offset-key="96968406e45648909e9fd52a76ab08cc:3"> </span><span slate-leaf="true" offset-key="96968406e45648909e9fd52a76ab08cc:4">createCounter</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="96968406e45648909e9fd52a76ab08cc:5">();</span></span>

<span key="a80f76444b3646978f4b3345f17d7b6a"><span offset-key="a80f76444b3646978f4b3345f17d7b6a:0">console</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="a80f76444b3646978f4b3345f17d7b6a:1">.</span><span slate-leaf="true" offset-key="a80f76444b3646978f4b3345f17d7b6a:2">log</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="a80f76444b3646978f4b3345f17d7b6a:3">(</span><span slate-leaf="true" offset-key="a80f76444b3646978f4b3345f17d7b6a:4">counter2</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="a80f76444b3646978f4b3345f17d7b6a:5">());</span><span offset-key="a80f76444b3646978f4b3345f17d7b6a:6"> </span><span class="r-17y197c" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="a80f76444b3646978f4b3345f17d7b6a:7">// => 1</span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3NC05MTMyOF8iIGNsYXNzPSJyLWg3Z2RvYiByLTEwcHR1bjcgci0xdnppOHhpIiBzdHlsZT0id2lkdGg6MTZweCI+PHBhdGggZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBjbGlwLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGQ9Ik0wIC41QS41LjUgMCAwMS41IDBoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNVY0aC0xVjFIMXY5aDN2MUguNWEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUtLjVWLjV6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTUgNS41YS41LjUgMCAwMS41LS41aDEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS41LjV2MTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LjVoLTEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNXYtMTB6TTYgNnY5aDlWNkg2eiIgZmlsbD0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

Copied!

<span key="d4e60a28bcad4e329a828eab77db03ea"><span offset-key="d4e60a28bcad4e329a828eab77db03ea:0">In the above code we are storing the anonymous inner function inside the </span>`createCounter`<span offset-key="d4e60a28bcad4e329a828eab77db03ea:2"> function onto the variable </span>`counter`<span offset-key="d4e60a28bcad4e329a828eab77db03ea:4">. The </span>`counter`<span offset-key="d4e60a28bcad4e329a828eab77db03ea:6"> variable is now a </span>*closure*<span offset-key="d4e60a28bcad4e329a828eab77db03ea:8">. The </span>`counter`<span offset-key="d4e60a28bcad4e329a828eab77db03ea:10"> variable </span>**closes over**<span offset-key="d4e60a28bcad4e329a828eab77db03ea:12"> the inner </span>`count`<span offset-key="d4e60a28bcad4e329a828eab77db03ea:14"> value inside </span>`createCounter`<span offset-key="d4e60a28bcad4e329a828eab77db03ea:16"> even after </span>`createCounter`<span offset-key="d4e60a28bcad4e329a828eab77db03ea:18"> has returned.</span></span>

<span key="3c089e119db04ed8999a8865188641d7"><span offset-key="3c089e119db04ed8999a8865188641d7:0">By </span>**closing over**<span offset-key="3c089e119db04ed8999a8865188641d7:2"> (or </span>**capturing**<span offset-key="3c089e119db04ed8999a8865188641d7:4">) the </span>`count`<span offset-key="3c089e119db04ed8999a8865188641d7:6"> variable, each function that is return from </span>`createCounter`<span offset-key="3c089e119db04ed8999a8865188641d7:8"> has a </span>**private**<span offset-key="3c089e119db04ed8999a8865188641d7:10">, mutable state that cannot be accessed externally. There is no way any outside function beside the closure itself can access the </span>`count`<span offset-key="3c089e119db04ed8999a8865188641d7:12"> state.</span></span>

### 

<span key="cae41ae986494a13bedfb63bd08629e9"><span offset-key="cae41ae986494a13bedfb63bd08629e9:0">Passing Arguments Implicitly</span></span>

<span key="4d8529c7aae74d6fa032f42ae2911cac"><span offset-key="4d8529c7aae74d6fa032f42ae2911cac:0">How to implement a closure and explain how that closure effects scope.</span></span>

# 

<span key="84bea68b8a274ea29ab5d261d7030a0a"><span offset-key="84bea68b8a274ea29ab5d261d7030a0a:0">Context in JavaScript</span></span>

<span key="d31c679239fe4a01b0d85d3d0edaaee8"><span offset-key="d31c679239fe4a01b0d85d3d0edaaee8:0">It's now time to dive into one of the most interesting concepts in JavaScript: the idea of </span>**context**<span offset-key="d31c679239fe4a01b0d85d3d0edaaee8:2">.</span></span>

<span key="0b89454442714bf1beeb89ab45862cea"><span offset-key="0b89454442714bf1beeb89ab45862cea:0">Programmers from the junior to senior level often confuse </span>*scope*<span offset-key="0b89454442714bf1beeb89ab45862cea:2"> and </span>*context*<span offset-key="0b89454442714bf1beeb89ab45862cea:4"> as the same thing - but that is not the case! Every function that is invoked has </span>**both**<span offset-key="0b89454442714bf1beeb89ab45862cea:6"> a scope and a context associated with that function. </span>*Scope*<span offset-key="0b89454442714bf1beeb89ab45862cea:8"> refers to the visibility and availability of variables, whereas </span>*context*<span offset-key="0b89454442714bf1beeb89ab45862cea:10"> refers to the value of the </span>`this`<span offset-key="0b89454442714bf1beeb89ab45862cea:12"> keyword when code is executed.</span></span>

<span key="f7a0a42446a2465aa79a9f0e0ac3be15"><span offset-key="f7a0a42446a2465aa79a9f0e0ac3be15:0">When you finish this reading you should be able to:</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="07d4e90ee4e844e1bb37aa0274310fbd"><span offset-key="07d4e90ee4e844e1bb37aa0274310fbd:0">Define a method that references </span>`this`<span offset-key="07d4e90ee4e844e1bb37aa0274310fbd:2"> on an object</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="0938ebe093c949a8a849fe9a9d715f71"><span offset-key="0938ebe093c949a8a849fe9a9d715f71:0">Identify what </span>`this`<span offset-key="0938ebe093c949a8a849fe9a9d715f71:2"> refers to in a code snippet</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="04f6fcf8b82a4253b9169dc3b07eae63"><span offset-key="04f6fcf8b82a4253b9169dc3b07eae63:0">Utilize the built in </span>`Function#bind`<span offset-key="04f6fcf8b82a4253b9169dc3b07eae63:2"> to maintain the context of </span>`this`</span>

## 

<span key="d8a54444406d45d994d31cb5ffc79331"><span offset-key="d8a54444406d45d994d31cb5ffc79331:0">What about </span>`this`<span offset-key="d8a54444406d45d994d31cb5ffc79331:2">?</span></span>

<span key="886a4c035df844029a4a9ed072f74125"><span offset-key="886a4c035df844029a4a9ed072f74125:0">When learning about objects we previously came across the idea of a </span>*method*<span offset-key="886a4c035df844029a4a9ed072f74125:2">. A </span>*method*<span offset-key="886a4c035df844029a4a9ed072f74125:4"> is a function that is a value within an object and belongs to an object.</span></span>

<span key="92cf18765da9425ba3f612a4ac5f939e"><span offset-key="92cf18765da9425ba3f612a4ac5f939e:0">There will be times when you will have to know which object a method belongs to. The keyword </span>`this`<span offset-key="92cf18765da9425ba3f612a4ac5f939e:2"> exists in every function and it evaluates to the object that is currently invoking that function. So the value of </span>`this`<span offset-key="92cf18765da9425ba3f612a4ac5f939e:4"> relies entirely on </span>**where**<span offset-key="92cf18765da9425ba3f612a4ac5f939e:6"> a function is invoked.</span></span>

<span key="6dc73db04aba41c1917f38c1bb7bec93"><span offset-key="6dc73db04aba41c1917f38c1bb7bec93:0">That may sound pretty abstract, so let's jump into an example:</span></span>

1

<span key="50f7c8f76ec540b6a4889b10d2dc128d"><span class="r-y7gyvo" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="50f7c8f76ec540b6a4889b10d2dc128d:0">let</span><span offset-key="50f7c8f76ec540b6a4889b10d2dc128d:1"> dog </span><span class="r-11faab8" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="50f7c8f76ec540b6a4889b10d2dc128d:2">=</span><span offset-key="50f7c8f76ec540b6a4889b10d2dc128d:3"> </span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="50f7c8f76ec540b6a4889b10d2dc128d:4">{</span></span>

2

Copied!

<span key="fac271593b4c48878df295c3fc61070d"><span offset-key="fac271593b4c48878df295c3fc61070d:0">Inside of a method, we can use the keyword </span>`this`<span offset-key="fac271593b4c48878df295c3fc61070d:2"> to refer to the object that is calling that method! So when calling </span>`dog.stand()`<span offset-key="fac271593b4c48878df295c3fc61070d:4"> and we invoke the code of the </span>`stand`<span offset-key="fac271593b4c48878df295c3fc61070d:6"> method, </span>`this`<span offset-key="fac271593b4c48878df295c3fc61070d:8"> will refer to the </span>`dog`<span offset-key="fac271593b4c48878df295c3fc61070d:10"> object.</span></span>

<span key="230a109c617942d680a0b3fa049ca4c1"><span offset-key="230a109c617942d680a0b3fa049ca4c1:0">Still skeptical? Don't take our word for it, check </span>`this`<span offset-key="230a109c617942d680a0b3fa049ca4c1:2"> (heh) out:</span></span>

<span key="abffbba0197c4af9aad0c0379acfbea4"><span offset-key="abffbba0197c4af9aad0c0379acfbea4:0">In short, by using the </span>`this`<span offset-key="abffbba0197c4af9aad0c0379acfbea4:2"> keyword inside a method, we can refer to values within that object.</span></span>

<span key="bae02a715a4d469187f11bc67a691b7a"><span offset-key="bae02a715a4d469187f11bc67a691b7a:0">Let's look at another example of this:</span></span>

<span key="330c30b9c5fe4f78abd693b8982db55a"><span offset-key="330c30b9c5fe4f78abd693b8982db55a:0"><span slate-zero-width="n">​</span></span></span>

10

<span key="b6e174a9c4c54f07aabb03fa39a6f055"><span offset-key="b6e174a9c4c54f07aabb03fa39a6f055:0">cat</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="b6e174a9c4c54f07aabb03fa39a6f055:1">.</span><span slate-leaf="true" offset-key="b6e174a9c4c54f07aabb03fa39a6f055:2">purrMore</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="b6e174a9c4c54f07aabb03fa39a6f055:3">();</span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3NC05MTMyOF8iIGNsYXNzPSJyLWg3Z2RvYiByLTEwcHR1bjcgci0xdnppOHhpIiBzdHlsZT0id2lkdGg6MTZweCI+PHBhdGggZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBjbGlwLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGQ9Ik0wIC41QS41LjUgMCAwMS41IDBoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNVY0aC0xVjFIMXY5aDN2MUguNWEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUtLjVWLjV6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTUgNS41YS41LjUgMCAwMS41LS41aDEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS41LjV2MTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LjVoLTEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNXYtMTB6TTYgNnY5aDlWNkg2eiIgZmlsbD0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

Copied!

<span key="d92bc399c402492089a7dd76122d8bed"><span offset-key="d92bc399c402492089a7dd76122d8bed:0">Through the </span>`this`<span offset-key="d92bc399c402492089a7dd76122d8bed:2"> variable, the </span>`purrMore`<span offset-key="d92bc399c402492089a7dd76122d8bed:4"> method can access the object it was called on. In </span>`purrMore`<span offset-key="d92bc399c402492089a7dd76122d8bed:6">, we use </span>`this`<span offset-key="d92bc399c402492089a7dd76122d8bed:8"> to access the </span>`cat`<span offset-key="d92bc399c402492089a7dd76122d8bed:10"> object that has a </span>`purr`<span offset-key="d92bc399c402492089a7dd76122d8bed:12"> method. In other words, inside of the </span>`purrMore`<span offset-key="d92bc399c402492089a7dd76122d8bed:14"> function if we had tried to use </span>`purr()`<span offset-key="d92bc399c402492089a7dd76122d8bed:16"> instead of </span>`this.purr()`<span offset-key="d92bc399c402492089a7dd76122d8bed:18"> it would not work.</span></span>

<span key="6e0fa18fb1fe4c06aa089856f1e7cd34"><span offset-key="6e0fa18fb1fe4c06aa089856f1e7cd34:0">When we invoked the </span>`purrMore`<span offset-key="6e0fa18fb1fe4c06aa089856f1e7cd34:2"> function using </span>`cat.purrMore`<span offset-key="6e0fa18fb1fe4c06aa089856f1e7cd34:4"> we used a </span>**method-style**<span offset-key="6e0fa18fb1fe4c06aa089856f1e7cd34:6"> invocation.</span></span>

<span key="499d10ebe1c74007963fbc3625818bf2"><span offset-key="499d10ebe1c74007963fbc3625818bf2:0">Method style invocations follow the format: </span>`object.method(args)`<span offset-key="499d10ebe1c74007963fbc3625818bf2:2">. You've already been doing this using built in data type methods! (i.e. </span>`Array#push`<span offset-key="499d10ebe1c74007963fbc3625818bf2:4">, </span>`String#toUpperCase`<span offset-key="499d10ebe1c74007963fbc3625818bf2:6">, etc.)</span></span>

<span key="b04713b12ae84984ae23eeebe0ac00d8"><span offset-key="b04713b12ae84984ae23eeebe0ac00d8:0">Using </span>*method-style invocation*<span offset-key="b04713b12ae84984ae23eeebe0ac00d8:2"> (note the </span>*dot notation*<span offset-key="b04713b12ae84984ae23eeebe0ac00d8:4">) ensures the method will be invoked and that the </span>`this`<span offset-key="b04713b12ae84984ae23eeebe0ac00d8:6"> within the method will be the object that method was called upon.</span></span>

<span key="a4e6425bcb51470fb0b56901051ffcf6"><span offset-key="a4e6425bcb51470fb0b56901051ffcf6:0">Now that we have gone over what </span>`this`<span offset-key="a4e6425bcb51470fb0b56901051ffcf6:2"> refers to - you can have a full understanding of the definition of context. </span>**Context refers to the value of** **`this`** **within a function and** **`this`** **refers to where a function is invoked**<span offset-key="a4e6425bcb51470fb0b56901051ffcf6:8">.</span></span>

## 

<span key="29072a9642524ef783546e1a1ccf97f9"><span offset-key="29072a9642524ef783546e1a1ccf97f9:0">Issues with scope and context</span></span>

<span key="88952e262936474b8e36512786cb44c2"><span offset-key="88952e262936474b8e36512786cb44c2:0">In the case of context the value of </span>`this`<span offset-key="88952e262936474b8e36512786cb44c2:2"> is determined by </span>*how*<span offset-key="88952e262936474b8e36512786cb44c2:4"> a function is invoked. In the above section we talked briefly about </span>*method-style invocation*<span offset-key="88952e262936474b8e36512786cb44c2:6">, where </span>`this`<span offset-key="88952e262936474b8e36512786cb44c2:8"> is set to the object the method was called upon.</span></span>

<span key="03933b15755140dc8728fd10b44a60ce"><span offset-key="03933b15755140dc8728fd10b44a60ce:0">Let's now talk about what </span>`this`<span offset-key="03933b15755140dc8728fd10b44a60ce:2"> is when using normal </span>*function style invocation*<span offset-key="03933b15755140dc8728fd10b44a60ce:4">.</span></span>

<span key="984480e2dda54236a8d12520fa7c3392"><span offset-key="984480e2dda54236a8d12520fa7c3392:0">If you run the following in Node:</span></span>

1

<span key="e8806c9bada44411a031947c00b3d613"><span class="r-y7gyvo" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="e8806c9bada44411a031947c00b3d613:0">function</span><span offset-key="e8806c9bada44411a031947c00b3d613:1"> </span><span slate-leaf="true" offset-key="e8806c9bada44411a031947c00b3d613:2">testMe</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="e8806c9bada44411a031947c00b3d613:3">()</span><span offset-key="e8806c9bada44411a031947c00b3d613:4"> </span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="e8806c9bada44411a031947c00b3d613:5">{</span></span>

2

<span key="bfcd5c6035b74cf4a76f430c975210a1"><span offset-key="bfcd5c6035b74cf4a76f430c975210a1:0"> console</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="bfcd5c6035b74cf4a76f430c975210a1:1">.</span><span slate-leaf="true" offset-key="bfcd5c6035b74cf4a76f430c975210a1:2">log</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="bfcd5c6035b74cf4a76f430c975210a1:3">(</span><span class="r-y7gyvo" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="bfcd5c6035b74cf4a76f430c975210a1:4">this</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="bfcd5c6035b74cf4a76f430c975210a1:5">);</span><span offset-key="bfcd5c6035b74cf4a76f430c975210a1:6"> </span><span class="r-17y197c" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="bfcd5c6035b74cf4a76f430c975210a1:7">//</span></span>

Copied!

<span key="6aa27e8daa89478f8eab9834c3e4e512"><span offset-key="6aa27e8daa89478f8eab9834c3e4e512:0">When you run the above </span>`testMe`<span offset-key="6aa27e8daa89478f8eab9834c3e4e512:2"> function in Node you'll see that </span>`this`<span offset-key="6aa27e8daa89478f8eab9834c3e4e512:4"> is set to the </span>`global`<span offset-key="6aa27e8daa89478f8eab9834c3e4e512:6"> object. To reiterate: each function you invoke will have </span>*both*<span offset-key="6aa27e8daa89478f8eab9834c3e4e512:8"> a context and a scope. So even running functions in Node that are not defined explicitly on declared objects are run using the global object as their </span>`this`<span offset-key="6aa27e8daa89478f8eab9834c3e4e512:10"> and therefore their context.</span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3NC05MTMyOF8iIGNsYXNzPSJyLWg3Z2RvYiByLTEwcHR1bjcgci0xdnppOHhpIiBzdHlsZT0id2lkdGg6MTZweCI+PHBhdGggZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBjbGlwLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGQ9Ik0wIC41QS41LjUgMCAwMS41IDBoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNVY0aC0xVjFIMXY5aDN2MUguNWEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUtLjVWLjV6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTUgNS41YS41LjUgMCAwMS41LS41aDEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS41LjV2MTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LjVoLTEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNXYtMTB6TTYgNnY5aDlWNkg2eiIgZmlsbD0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

Copied!

<span key="d0605adfed624a5bb9885ecee76b98a3"><span offset-key="d0605adfed624a5bb9885ecee76b98a3:0">So in the above code notice how we stored the </span>`dog.changeName`<span offset-key="d0605adfed624a5bb9885ecee76b98a3:2"> function </span>*without invoking it*<span offset-key="d0605adfed624a5bb9885ecee76b98a3:4"> to the variable </span>`change`<span offset-key="d0605adfed624a5bb9885ecee76b98a3:6">. On the next line when we did invoke the </span>`change`<span offset-key="d0605adfed624a5bb9885ecee76b98a3:8"> function we can see that we did not actually change the </span>`dog`<span offset-key="d0605adfed624a5bb9885ecee76b98a3:10"> object like we intended to. We created a new key value pair for </span>`name`<span offset-key="d0605adfed624a5bb9885ecee76b98a3:12"> on the global object! This is because we invoked change without the context of a specific object (like </span>`dog`<span offset-key="d0605adfed624a5bb9885ecee76b98a3:14">), so JavaScript used the only object available to it, the </span>**global object**<span offset-key="d0605adfed624a5bb9885ecee76b98a3:16">!</span></span>

<span key="5645127e2fa5408f8c2592c9c3752500"><span offset-key="5645127e2fa5408f8c2592c9c3752500:0">The above example might seem like an annoying inconvenience but let's take a look at what happens when calling something in the wrong context can be a big problem.</span></span>

<span key="060f5f98ccf947ee82558c24ade39db7"><span offset-key="060f5f98ccf947ee82558c24ade39db7:0">Using our </span>`cat`<span offset-key="060f5f98ccf947ee82558c24ade39db7:2"> object from before:</span></span>

<span key="f75c554a1f24423c9ed3c4d19b05d163"><span offset-key="f75c554a1f24423c9ed3c4d19b05d163:0">console</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="f75c554a1f24423c9ed3c4d19b05d163:1">.</span><span slate-leaf="true" offset-key="f75c554a1f24423c9ed3c4d19b05d163:2">log</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="f75c554a1f24423c9ed3c4d19b05d163:3">(</span><span slate-leaf="true" offset-key="f75c554a1f24423c9ed3c4d19b05d163:4">notACat</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="f75c554a1f24423c9ed3c4d19b05d163:5">());</span><span offset-key="f75c554a1f24423c9ed3c4d19b05d163:6"> </span><span class="r-17y197c" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="f75c554a1f24423c9ed3c4d19b05d163:7">// TypeError: this.purr is not a function</span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3NC05MTMyOF8iIGNsYXNzPSJyLWg3Z2RvYiByLTEwcHR1bjcgci0xdnppOHhpIiBzdHlsZT0id2lkdGg6MTZweCI+PHBhdGggZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBjbGlwLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGQ9Ik0wIC41QS41LjUgMCAwMS41IDBoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNVY0aC0xVjFIMXY5aDN2MUguNWEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUtLjVWLjV6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTUgNS41YS41LjUgMCAwMS41LS41aDEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS41LjV2MTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LjVoLTEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNXYtMTB6TTYgNnY5aDlWNkg2eiIgZmlsbD0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

Copied!

<span key="51f8432c73fb4cea86ee493a2818c944"><span offset-key="51f8432c73fb4cea86ee493a2818c944:0">So in the above code snippet we attempted to call the </span>`purrMore`<span offset-key="51f8432c73fb4cea86ee493a2818c944:2"> function </span>*without the correct Object for context*<span offset-key="51f8432c73fb4cea86ee493a2818c944:4">. Meaning we attempted to call the </span>`purrMore`<span offset-key="51f8432c73fb4cea86ee493a2818c944:6"> function on the global object! Since the global object does not have a </span>`purr`<span offset-key="51f8432c73fb4cea86ee493a2818c944:8"> method upon its </span>`this`<span offset-key="51f8432c73fb4cea86ee493a2818c944:10"> it raised an error. This is a common problem when invoking methods: invoking methods without their proper context.</span></span>

<span key="abee3428c5854c7f8224acabde3bb38b"><span offset-key="abee3428c5854c7f8224acabde3bb38b:0">Let's look at one more example of confusing </span>`this`<span offset-key="abee3428c5854c7f8224acabde3bb38b:2"> when using a callback. Incorrectly passing context is an inherent problem with callbacks. The </span>`global.setTimeout()`<span offset-key="abee3428c5854c7f8224acabde3bb38b:4"> method on the global object is a popular way of setting a function to run on a timer. The </span>`global.setTimeout()`<span offset-key="abee3428c5854c7f8224acabde3bb38b:6"> method accepts a callback and a number of milliseconds to wait before invoking the callback.</span></span>

<span key="992088c417594723b8c6be76f56793b7"><span offset-key="992088c417594723b8c6be76f56793b7:0">Let's look at a simple example:</span></span>

1

<span key="b1e9ee62d100418ab24a3d77040da5cb"><span class="r-y7gyvo" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="b1e9ee62d100418ab24a3d77040da5cb:0">let</span><span offset-key="b1e9ee62d100418ab24a3d77040da5cb:1"> </span><span slate-leaf="true" offset-key="b1e9ee62d100418ab24a3d77040da5cb:2">hello</span><span offset-key="b1e9ee62d100418ab24a3d77040da5cb:3"> </span><span class="r-11faab8" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="b1e9ee62d100418ab24a3d77040da5cb:4">=</span><span offset-key="b1e9ee62d100418ab24a3d77040da5cb:5"> </span><span class="r-y7gyvo" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="b1e9ee62d100418ab24a3d77040da5cb:6">function</span><span offset-key="b1e9ee62d100418ab24a3d77040da5cb:7"> </span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="b1e9ee62d100418ab24a3d77040da5cb:8">()</span><span offset-key="b1e9ee62d100418ab24a3d77040da5cb:9"> </span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="b1e9ee62d100418ab24a3d77040da5cb:10">{</span></span>

<span key="ab12dd28bcec45b793c6fda7b19bb12f"><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="ab12dd28bcec45b793c6fda7b19bb12f:0">};</span></span>

<span key="f6725ab566484f51a91c91c7d8656ec9"><span offset-key="f6725ab566484f51a91c91c7d8656ec9:0"><span slate-zero-width="n">​</span></span></span>

<span key="ae7cb261f9e34c6ca318227dfb373581"><span class="r-17y197c" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="ae7cb261f9e34c6ca318227dfb373581:0">// global. is a method of the global object!</span></span>

<span key="bdfa591956e04cc28b8ba76cc305db2e"><span offset-key="bdfa591956e04cc28b8ba76cc305db2e:0">global</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="bdfa591956e04cc28b8ba76cc305db2e:1">.</span><span slate-leaf="true" offset-key="bdfa591956e04cc28b8ba76cc305db2e:2">setTimeout</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="bdfa591956e04cc28b8ba76cc305db2e:3">(</span><span offset-key="bdfa591956e04cc28b8ba76cc305db2e:4">hello</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="bdfa591956e04cc28b8ba76cc305db2e:5">,</span><span offset-key="bdfa591956e04cc28b8ba76cc305db2e:6"> </span><span class="r-11faab8" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="bdfa591956e04cc28b8ba76cc305db2e:7">5000</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="bdfa591956e04cc28b8ba76cc305db2e:8">);</span><span offset-key="bdfa591956e04cc28b8ba76cc305db2e:9"> </span><span class="r-17y197c" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="bdfa591956e04cc28b8ba76cc305db2e:10">// waits 5 seconds then prints "hello!"</span></span>

<span key="349632b0e5ea4f7d9637e6c9e4ff7c8a"><span offset-key="349632b0e5ea4f7d9637e6c9e4ff7c8a:0"><span slate-zero-width="n">​</span></span></span>

<span key="390f6fe5377c4b05ae7899021b288665"><span offset-key="390f6fe5377c4b05ae7899021b288665:0">global</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="390f6fe5377c4b05ae7899021b288665:1">.</span><span slate-leaf="true" offset-key="390f6fe5377c4b05ae7899021b288665:2">setTimeout</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="390f6fe5377c4b05ae7899021b288665:3">(</span><span offset-key="390f6fe5377c4b05ae7899021b288665:4">cat</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="390f6fe5377c4b05ae7899021b288665:5">.</span><span offset-key="390f6fe5377c4b05ae7899021b288665:6">purrMore</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="390f6fe5377c4b05ae7899021b288665:7">,</span><span offset-key="390f6fe5377c4b05ae7899021b288665:8"> </span><span class="r-11faab8" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="390f6fe5377c4b05ae7899021b288665:9">5000</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="390f6fe5377c4b05ae7899021b288665:10">);</span><span offset-key="390f6fe5377c4b05ae7899021b288665:11"> </span><span class="r-17y197c" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="390f6fe5377c4b05ae7899021b288665:12">// 5 seconds later: TypeError: this.purr is not a function</span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3NC05MTMyOF8iIGNsYXNzPSJyLWg3Z2RvYiByLTEwcHR1bjcgci0xdnppOHhpIiBzdHlsZT0id2lkdGg6MTZweCI+PHBhdGggZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBjbGlwLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGQ9Ik0wIC41QS41LjUgMCAwMS41IDBoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNVY0aC0xVjFIMXY5aDN2MUguNWEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUtLjVWLjV6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTUgNS41YS41LjUgMCAwMS41LS41aDEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS41LjV2MTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LjVoLTEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNXYtMTB6TTYgNnY5aDlWNkg2eiIgZmlsbD0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

Copied!

<span key="676515d1d1714fcc8a9ca8162054ff52"><span offset-key="676515d1d1714fcc8a9ca8162054ff52:0">So what happened there? We called </span>`cat.purrMore`<span offset-key="676515d1d1714fcc8a9ca8162054ff52:2"> so it should have the right context right? Noooooope. This is because </span>`cat.purrMore`<span offset-key="676515d1d1714fcc8a9ca8162054ff52:4"> is a callback in the above code! Meaning that when the </span>`global.setTimeout`<span offset-key="676515d1d1714fcc8a9ca8162054ff52:6"> function attempts to call the </span>`purrMore`<span offset-key="676515d1d1714fcc8a9ca8162054ff52:8"> function all it has reference to is the function itself. Since </span>`setTimeout`<span offset-key="676515d1d1714fcc8a9ca8162054ff52:10"> is on the global object that means that the global object will be the context for attempting to invoke the </span>`cat.purrMore`<span offset-key="676515d1d1714fcc8a9ca8162054ff52:12"> function.</span></span>

<span key="182024cf98aa480bac3e3e690d307c11">**Strictly protecting the global object**</span>

<span key="bb5187066bbe4da7aca2f1a87758259e"><span offset-key="bb5187066bbe4da7aca2f1a87758259e:0">The accidental mutation of the global object when invoking functions in unintended contexts is one of the reasons JavaScript released "strict" mode in ECMAScript version 5. We won't dive too much into JavaScript's strict mode here, but it's important to know how strict mode can be used to protect the global object.</span></span>

<span key="fb4ca22e82e444b9a33100bb89c85f84"><span offset-key="fb4ca22e82e444b9a33100bb89c85f84:0">Writing and running code in strict mode is easy and much like writing code in "sloppy mode" (jargon for the normal JavaScript environment). We can run JavaScript in strict mode simply by adding the string "use strict" at the top of our file:</span></span>

1

<span key="2c40a1b4f72f4613870149965548753d"><span class="r-qtrn9a" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="2c40a1b4f72f4613870149965548753d:0">"use strict"</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="2c40a1b4f72f4613870149965548753d:1">;</span></span>

2

<span key="b04ac4b523ed42a5940682db4578050c"><span offset-key="b04ac4b523ed42a5940682db4578050c:0"><span slate-zero-width="n">​</span></span></span>

Copied!

<span key="4743e2bbe5684b3cad8e85d5a6cddde3"><span offset-key="4743e2bbe5684b3cad8e85d5a6cddde3:0">One of the differences of strict mode becomes apparent when trying to access the global object. As we mentioned previously, the global object is the context of invoked functions in Node that are not defined explicitly on declared objects.</span></span>

<span key="fbda9b7372274006973708a18da3a169"><span offset-key="fbda9b7372274006973708a18da3a169:0">So referencing </span>`this`<span offset-key="fbda9b7372274006973708a18da3a169:2"> within a function using the global object as its context will give us access to the global object:</span></span>

1

<span key="7677e26b287840a0a6a00a155ea3a06b"><span class="r-y7gyvo" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="7677e26b287840a0a6a00a155ea3a06b:0">function</span><span offset-key="7677e26b287840a0a6a00a155ea3a06b:1"> </span><span slate-leaf="true" offset-key="7677e26b287840a0a6a00a155ea3a06b:2">hello</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="7677e26b287840a0a6a00a155ea3a06b:3">()</span><span offset-key="7677e26b287840a0a6a00a155ea3a06b:4"> </span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="7677e26b287840a0a6a00a155ea3a06b:5">{</span></span>

<span key="ddb5220f121c43ab82d981a4df248228"><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="ddb5220f121c43ab82d981a4df248228:0">}</span></span>

Copied!

<span key="7d69edf686624c18b17601a2dc46da5b"><span offset-key="7d69edf686624c18b17601a2dc46da5b:0">However, strict mode will no longer allow you access to the global object in functions via the </span>`this`<span offset-key="7d69edf686624c18b17601a2dc46da5b:2"> keyword and will instead return </span>`undefined`<span offset-key="7d69edf686624c18b17601a2dc46da5b:4">:</span></span>

1

<span key="d8e0e1431dc44b53a522cf3d03d23ea0"><span class="r-qtrn9a" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="d8e0e1431dc44b53a522cf3d03d23ea0:0">"use strict"</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="d8e0e1431dc44b53a522cf3d03d23ea0:1">;</span></span>

2

<span key="d00e9201286b4ef3987e07cbad2e1562"><span offset-key="d00e9201286b4ef3987e07cbad2e1562:0"><span slate-zero-width="n">​</span></span></span>

<span key="0a18259be36f47a3afcb7bbe6a93d39b"><span offset-key="0a18259be36f47a3afcb7bbe6a93d39b:0"> console</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="0a18259be36f47a3afcb7bbe6a93d39b:1">.</span><span slate-leaf="true" offset-key="0a18259be36f47a3afcb7bbe6a93d39b:2">log</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="0a18259be36f47a3afcb7bbe6a93d39b:3">(</span><span class="r-y7gyvo" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="0a18259be36f47a3afcb7bbe6a93d39b:4">this</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="0a18259be36f47a3afcb7bbe6a93d39b:5">);</span></span>

<span key="9ea30da7b2c843f080f824fdffd6ab80"><span offset-key="9ea30da7b2c843f080f824fdffd6ab80:0">Using strict mode can help us avoid scenarios where we accidentally would have mutated the global object. Let's take our example from earlier and try it in strict mode:</span></span>

<span key="526023f4686d4fd8b14573fb79db7402"><span class="r-y7gyvo" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="526023f4686d4fd8b14573fb79db7402:0">let</span><span offset-key="526023f4686d4fd8b14573fb79db7402:1"> changeNameFunc </span><span class="r-11faab8" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="526023f4686d4fd8b14573fb79db7402:2">=</span><span offset-key="526023f4686d4fd8b14573fb79db7402:3"> dog</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="526023f4686d4fd8b14573fb79db7402:4">.</span><span offset-key="526023f4686d4fd8b14573fb79db7402:5">changeName</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="526023f4686d4fd8b14573fb79db7402:6">;</span></span>
