<span key="648cc1ed8bf844599350cded79b6834c"><span offset-key="648cc1ed8bf844599350cded79b6834c:0">console</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="648cc1ed8bf844599350cded79b6834c:1">.</span><span slate-leaf="true" offset-key="648cc1ed8bf844599350cded79b6834c:2">log</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="648cc1ed8bf844599350cded79b6834c:3">(</span><span slate-leaf="true" offset-key="648cc1ed8bf844599350cded79b6834c:4">changeNameFunc</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="648cc1ed8bf844599350cded79b6834c:5">());</span><span offset-key="648cc1ed8bf844599350cded79b6834c:6"> </span><span class="r-17y197c" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="648cc1ed8bf844599350cded79b6834c:7">// TypeError: Cannot set property 'name' of undefined</span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3NC05MTMyOF8iIGNsYXNzPSJyLWg3Z2RvYiByLTEwcHR1bjcgci0xdnppOHhpIiBzdHlsZT0id2lkdGg6MTZweCI+PHBhdGggZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBjbGlwLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGQ9Ik0wIC41QS41LjUgMCAwMS41IDBoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNVY0aC0xVjFIMXY5aDN2MUguNWEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUtLjVWLjV6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTUgNS41YS41LjUgMCAwMS41LS41aDEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS41LjV2MTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LjVoLTEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNXYtMTB6TTYgNnY5aDlWNkg2eiIgZmlsbD0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

Copied!

<span key="68bdaf9a35c6472a9773fba112f135f9"><span offset-key="68bdaf9a35c6472a9773fba112f135f9:0">As you can see above, when we attempt to invoke the </span>`changeNameFunc`<span offset-key="68bdaf9a35c6472a9773fba112f135f9:2"> an error is thrown because referencing </span>`this`<span offset-key="68bdaf9a35c6472a9773fba112f135f9:4"> in strict mode will give us </span>`undefined`<span offset-key="68bdaf9a35c6472a9773fba112f135f9:6"> instead of the global object. The above behavior is helpful for catching otherwise tricky bugs.</span></span>

<span key="104951bc79c34c3aa86daeaecea1c6e3"><span offset-key="104951bc79c34c3aa86daeaecea1c6e3:0">If you'd like to learn more about strict mode we recommend checking out the </span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Strict_mode" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="f5bc240081104645b383ff1ceeed4d4e" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-91324_259-91325-237__"><span data-key="15010c68c46c4df98e80004e1dbaeca4"><span data-offset-key="15010c68c46c4df98e80004e1dbaeca4:0">documentation</span></span></span></a><span key="e21dbce6c7fe4ba8bdbab11ca12e35dc"><span offset-key="e21dbce6c7fe4ba8bdbab11ca12e35dc:0">.</span></span>

## 

<span key="a050a676b272402abe50e3eab15d97aa"><span offset-key="a050a676b272402abe50e3eab15d97aa:0">Changing context using </span>`bind`</span>

<span key="220d3a6246434594b642d9ec25a3fcb7"><span offset-key="220d3a6246434594b642d9ec25a3fcb7:0">Good thing JavaScript has something that can solve this problem for us: what is known as the </span>**binding**<span offset-key="220d3a6246434594b642d9ec25a3fcb7:2"> of a context to a function.</span></span>

<span key="98687039118846a7aa3469c6fa62c8f0"><span offset-key="98687039118846a7aa3469c6fa62c8f0:0">From the </span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Global_objects/Function/bind" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="8fc450633c524a03b6b5ba8ba5783a59" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-91324_259-91325-237__"><span data-key="3fac0f38f77b4a94bbbb95bdea2a60dc"><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="3fac0f38f77b4a94bbbb95bdea2a60dc:0">Function.prototype.bind()</code></span></span></a><span key="ca12b8f2eccd422b92c796042db6d828"><span offset-key="ca12b8f2eccd422b92c796042db6d828:0">, "The simplest use of </span>`bind()`<span offset-key="ca12b8f2eccd422b92c796042db6d828:2"> is to make a function that, no matter how it is called, is called with a particular </span>`this`<span offset-key="ca12b8f2eccd422b92c796042db6d828:4"> value".</span></span>

<span key="439fe46a014f4ce7a45646c852e57850"><span offset-key="439fe46a014f4ce7a45646c852e57850:0">Here is a preview of the syntax we use to </span>`bind`<span offset-key="439fe46a014f4ce7a45646c852e57850:2">:</span></span>

1

<span key="1dd0fe6271c044d9a1b2b4658ef61204"><span class="r-y7gyvo" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="1dd0fe6271c044d9a1b2b4658ef61204:0">let</span><span offset-key="1dd0fe6271c044d9a1b2b4658ef61204:1"> aboundFunc </span><span class="r-11faab8" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="1dd0fe6271c044d9a1b2b4658ef61204:2">=</span><span offset-key="1dd0fe6271c044d9a1b2b4658ef61204:3"> </span><span slate-leaf="true" offset-key="1dd0fe6271c044d9a1b2b4658ef61204:4">func</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="1dd0fe6271c044d9a1b2b4658ef61204:5">.</span><span slate-leaf="true" offset-key="1dd0fe6271c044d9a1b2b4658ef61204:6">bind</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="1dd0fe6271c044d9a1b2b4658ef61204:7">(</span><span offset-key="1dd0fe6271c044d9a1b2b4658ef61204:8">context</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="1dd0fe6271c044d9a1b2b4658ef61204:9">);</span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3NC05MTMyOF8iIGNsYXNzPSJyLWg3Z2RvYiByLTEwcHR1bjcgci0xdnppOHhpIiBzdHlsZT0id2lkdGg6MTZweCI+PHBhdGggZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBjbGlwLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGQ9Ik0wIC41QS41LjUgMCAwMS41IDBoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNVY0aC0xVjFIMXY5aDN2MUguNWEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUtLjVWLjV6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTUgNS41YS41LjUgMCAwMS41LS41aDEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS41LjV2MTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LjVoLTEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNXYtMTB6TTYgNnY5aDlWNkg2eiIgZmlsbD0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

Copied!

<span key="8e07c76728814030900ee95fd8ab69c1"><span offset-key="8e07c76728814030900ee95fd8ab69c1:0">So when we call </span>`bind`<span offset-key="8e07c76728814030900ee95fd8ab69c1:2"> we are returned what is called an exotic function. Which essentially means a function with it's </span>`this`<span offset-key="8e07c76728814030900ee95fd8ab69c1:4"> bound no matter where that function is invoked.</span></span>

<span key="33656168e80b402e86df0729c35bd829"><span offset-key="33656168e80b402e86df0729c35bd829:0">Let's take a look at example at </span>`bind`<span offset-key="33656168e80b402e86df0729c35bd829:2"> in action:</span></span>

1

<span key="0c25d4948154480db48f4a3df537850f"><span class="r-y7gyvo" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="0c25d4948154480db48f4a3df537850f:0">let</span><span offset-key="0c25d4948154480db48f4a3df537850f:1"> cat </span><span class="r-11faab8" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="0c25d4948154480db48f4a3df537850f:2">=</span><span offset-key="0c25d4948154480db48f4a3df537850f:3"> </span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="0c25d4948154480db48f4a3df537850f:4">{</span></span>

2

Copied!

<span key="3014cf1ffe3a4e79913585d117ca62c9"><span offset-key="3014cf1ffe3a4e79913585d117ca62c9:0">That is the magic of </span>`Function#bind`<span offset-key="3014cf1ffe3a4e79913585d117ca62c9:2">! It allows you choose the context for your function. You don't need to restrict the context you'd like to bind to either - you can </span>`bind`<span offset-key="3014cf1ffe3a4e79913585d117ca62c9:4"> functions to any context.</span></span>

<span key="55ba1214c0cb402ea9cd8c11c724f28e"><span offset-key="55ba1214c0cb402ea9cd8c11c724f28e:0">Let's look at another example:</span></span>

<span key="30271effa1414df595ce4f902112f85e">**Binding with arguments**</span>

<span key="3aaa348510c94b4585079ff7bdd86207"><span offset-key="3aaa348510c94b4585079ff7bdd86207:0">So far we've talking of one of the the common uses of the </span>`bind`<span offset-key="3aaa348510c94b4585079ff7bdd86207:2"> function - binding a context to a function. However, bind will not only allow you to bind the context of a function but also to bind </span>**arguments**<span offset-key="3aaa348510c94b4585079ff7bdd86207:4"> to a function.</span></span>

<span key="66a720fd20414e61b32b959c45cccc80"><span offset-key="66a720fd20414e61b32b959c45cccc80:0">Here is the syntax for binding arguments to a function:</span></span>

1

<span key="6c9033ff78494d629afb589f0c74ea84"><span class="r-y7gyvo" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="6c9033ff78494d629afb589f0c74ea84:0">let</span><span offset-key="6c9033ff78494d629afb589f0c74ea84:1"> aboundFunc </span><span class="r-11faab8" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="6c9033ff78494d629afb589f0c74ea84:2">=</span><span offset-key="6c9033ff78494d629afb589f0c74ea84:3"> </span><span slate-leaf="true" offset-key="6c9033ff78494d629afb589f0c74ea84:4">func</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="6c9033ff78494d629afb589f0c74ea84:5">.</span><span slate-leaf="true" offset-key="6c9033ff78494d629afb589f0c74ea84:6">bind</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="6c9033ff78494d629afb589f0c74ea84:7">(</span><span offset-key="6c9033ff78494d629afb589f0c74ea84:8">context</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="6c9033ff78494d629afb589f0c74ea84:9">,</span><span offset-key="6c9033ff78494d629afb589f0c74ea84:10"> arg1</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="6c9033ff78494d629afb589f0c74ea84:11">,</span><span offset-key="6c9033ff78494d629afb589f0c74ea84:12"> arg2</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="6c9033ff78494d629afb589f0c74ea84:13">,</span><span offset-key="6c9033ff78494d629afb589f0c74ea84:14"> etc</span><span class="r-11faab8" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="6c9033ff78494d629afb589f0c74ea84:15">...</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="6c9033ff78494d629afb589f0c74ea84:16">);</span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3NC05MTMyOF8iIGNsYXNzPSJyLWg3Z2RvYiByLTEwcHR1bjcgci0xdnppOHhpIiBzdHlsZT0id2lkdGg6MTZweCI+PHBhdGggZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBjbGlwLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGQ9Ik0wIC41QS41LjUgMCAwMS41IDBoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNVY0aC0xVjFIMXY5aDN2MUguNWEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUtLjVWLjV6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTUgNS41YS41LjUgMCAwMS41LS41aDEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS41LjV2MTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LjVoLTEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNXYtMTB6TTYgNnY5aDlWNkg2eiIgZmlsbD0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

<span key="e984246c017e411c8e326e55aa6fb722"><span offset-key="e984246c017e411c8e326e55aa6fb722:0">Following that train of logic let's look at example of binding arguments to a function, regardless of the context:</span></span>

1

<span key="3854e51539144cdb8618bb54556c2173"><span offset-key="3854e51539144cdb8618bb54556c2173:0">console</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="3854e51539144cdb8618bb54556c2173:1">.</span><span slate-leaf="true" offset-key="3854e51539144cdb8618bb54556c2173:2">log</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="3854e51539144cdb8618bb54556c2173:3">(</span><span slate-leaf="true" offset-key="3854e51539144cdb8618bb54556c2173:4">add3</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="3854e51539144cdb8618bb54556c2173:5">(</span><span class="r-11faab8" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="3854e51539144cdb8618bb54556c2173:6">10</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="3854e51539144cdb8618bb54556c2173:7">));</span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3NC05MTMyOF8iIGNsYXNzPSJyLWg3Z2RvYiByLTEwcHR1bjcgci0xdnppOHhpIiBzdHlsZT0id2lkdGg6MTZweCI+PHBhdGggZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBjbGlwLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGQ9Ik0wIC41QS41LjUgMCAwMS41IDBoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNVY0aC0xVjFIMXY5aDN2MUguNWEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUtLjVWLjV6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTUgNS41YS41LjUgMCAwMS41LS41aDEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS41LjV2MTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LjVoLTEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNXYtMTB6TTYgNnY5aDlWNkg2eiIgZmlsbD0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

Copied!

<span key="e9f27aff45d14ed2aceda8bf61e14eb3"><span offset-key="e9f27aff45d14ed2aceda8bf61e14eb3:0">Note that in the above snippet where we </span>`bind`<span offset-key="e9f27aff45d14ed2aceda8bf61e14eb3:2"> with </span>`null`<span offset-key="e9f27aff45d14ed2aceda8bf61e14eb3:4"> we don’t actually use </span>`this`<span offset-key="e9f27aff45d14ed2aceda8bf61e14eb3:6"> in the </span>`sum`<span offset-key="e9f27aff45d14ed2aceda8bf61e14eb3:8"> function. However, since </span>`bind`<span offset-key="e9f27aff45d14ed2aceda8bf61e14eb3:10"> requires a first argument we can put in </span>`null`<span offset-key="e9f27aff45d14ed2aceda8bf61e14eb3:12"> as a place holder.</span></span>

<span key="675d0d4ef52b4d2381a68761d21db21b"><span offset-key="675d0d4ef52b4d2381a68761d21db21b:0">Above when we created the </span>`add3`<span offset-key="675d0d4ef52b4d2381a68761d21db21b:2"> function we were creating a new bound function where the context was </span>`null`<span offset-key="675d0d4ef52b4d2381a68761d21db21b:4">, since the context won't matter, and the first argument will </span>*always*<span offset-key="675d0d4ef52b4d2381a68761d21db21b:6"> be </span>`3`<span offset-key="675d0d4ef52b4d2381a68761d21db21b:8"> for that function. Whenever we invoke the </span>`add3`<span offset-key="675d0d4ef52b4d2381a68761d21db21b:10"> function all other arguments will be passed in normally.</span></span>

<span key="59ceb35e496c4b05a0322bdd576ed85a"><span offset-key="59ceb35e496c4b05a0322bdd576ed85a:0">Using </span>`bind`<span offset-key="59ceb35e496c4b05a0322bdd576ed85a:2"> like this gives you a lot of flexibility with your code. Allowing you to create independent functions that essentially do the same thing while keeping your code very DRY.</span></span>

<span key="389fe6c3fd8544d5821f03d63bf0655a"><span offset-key="389fe6c3fd8544d5821f03d63bf0655a:0">Here is another example:</span></span>

# 

<span key="e550d3270d184d53bd1cb1b8f698ccc1"><span offset-key="e550d3270d184d53bd1cb1b8f698ccc1:0">Arrow Functions</span></span>

<span key="add7f71221e34205b784e20b3e1da9c9"><span offset-key="add7f71221e34205b784e20b3e1da9c9:0">Arrow functions, a.k.a. Fat Arrows (</span>`=>`<span offset-key="add7f71221e34205b784e20b3e1da9c9:2">), are a more concise way of declaring functions. Arrow functions were introduced in ES2015 as a way of solving many of the inconveniences of the normal callback function syntax.</span></span>

<span key="99981db90dbd40a98d1b502c38d2da62"><span offset-key="99981db90dbd40a98d1b502c38d2da62:0">Two major factors influenced the reason behind the desire for arrow functions: the need for shorter functions and behavior of </span>`this`<span offset-key="99981db90dbd40a98d1b502c38d2da62:2"> and context.</span></span>

<span key="7a94a317ce1f44b9a1eb9232bf907a85"><span offset-key="7a94a317ce1f44b9a1eb9232bf907a85:0">When you finish this reading you should be able to:</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="1f9ad2b8079046a08b2de2cea1665535"><span offset-key="1f9ad2b8079046a08b2de2cea1665535:0">Define an arrow function</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="d6f8a0061d0448ce953649ffdf23c477"><span offset-key="d6f8a0061d0448ce953649ffdf23c477:0">Given an arrow function, deduce the value of </span>`this`<span offset-key="d6f8a0061d0448ce953649ffdf23c477:2"> without executing the code</span></span>

<span key="9ccee4e44b8d44408ced107915fa42e3"><span offset-key="9ccee4e44b8d44408ced107915fa42e3:0">Both functions in the example above accomplish the same thing. However, the arrow syntax is a little shorter and easier to follow.</span></span>

### 

<span key="cf1cbbc2fb024acdb092cfd78d7b8dfa"><span offset-key="cf1cbbc2fb024acdb092cfd78d7b8dfa:0">Anatomy of an arrow function</span></span>

<span key="3e4c625128d4429fb92d4d814686aa94"><span offset-key="3e4c625128d4429fb92d4d814686aa94:0">The syntax for a multiple statement arrow function is as follows:</span></span>

1

<span key="1a111a5b34b34bc9911ea7a42cebf9e6"><span offset-key="1a111a5b34b34bc9911ea7a42cebf9e6:0">(parameters, go, here) => {</span></span>

2

<span key="4826c3e497b74033a8aee90423b7c8a8"><span offset-key="4826c3e497b74033a8aee90423b7c8a8:0"> statement1;</span></span>

3

<span key="b4c4e43e8b9a414f82522c8ec8ae104e"><span offset-key="b4c4e43e8b9a414f82522c8ec8ae104e:0"> statement2;</span></span>

4

<span key="3ca2a4f9f4164915ae0ea86eff759deb"><span offset-key="3ca2a4f9f4164915ae0ea86eff759deb:0"> return &lt;a value>;</span></span>

5

<span key="cc3731aac9bc4c0e868b0979fa5c0d29"><span offset-key="cc3731aac9bc4c0e868b0979fa5c0d29:0">}</span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3NC05MTMyOF8iIGNsYXNzPSJyLWg3Z2RvYiByLTEwcHR1bjcgci0xdnppOHhpIiBzdHlsZT0id2lkdGg6MTZweCI+PHBhdGggZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBjbGlwLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGQ9Ik0wIC41QS41LjUgMCAwMS41IDBoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNVY0aC0xVjFIMXY5aDN2MUguNWEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUtLjVWLjV6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTUgNS41YS41LjUgMCAwMS41LS41aDEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS41LjV2MTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LjVoLTEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNXYtMTB6TTYgNnY5aDlWNkg2eiIgZmlsbD0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

Copied!

<span key="ce9210a7d72e41eb84fa620738a9899b"><span offset-key="ce9210a7d72e41eb84fa620738a9899b:0">So let's look at a quick translation between a function declared with a function expression syntax and a fat arrow function. Take notice of the removal of the </span>`function`<span offset-key="ce9210a7d72e41eb84fa620738a9899b:2"> keyword, and the addition of the fat arrow (</span>`=>`<span offset-key="ce9210a7d72e41eb84fa620738a9899b:4">).</span></span>

1

<span key="96b328f002ae42e2b71aa5e1b5784f90"><span class="r-y7gyvo" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="96b328f002ae42e2b71aa5e1b5784f90:0">function</span><span offset-key="96b328f002ae42e2b71aa5e1b5784f90:1"> </span><span slate-leaf="true" offset-key="96b328f002ae42e2b71aa5e1b5784f90:2">fullName</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="96b328f002ae42e2b71aa5e1b5784f90:3">(</span><span slate-leaf="true" offset-key="96b328f002ae42e2b71aa5e1b5784f90:4">fname</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="96b328f002ae42e2b71aa5e1b5784f90:5">,</span><span slate-leaf="true" offset-key="96b328f002ae42e2b71aa5e1b5784f90:6"> lname</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="96b328f002ae42e2b71aa5e1b5784f90:7">)</span><span offset-key="96b328f002ae42e2b71aa5e1b5784f90:8"> </span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="96b328f002ae42e2b71aa5e1b5784f90:9">{</span></span>

2

<span key="63320f4f783e44658cce06bd6cbafdf9"><span offset-key="63320f4f783e44658cce06bd6cbafdf9:0"> </span><span class="r-y7gyvo" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="63320f4f783e44658cce06bd6cbafdf9:1">let</span><span offset-key="63320f4f783e44658cce06bd6cbafdf9:2"> str </span><span class="r-11faab8" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="63320f4f783e44658cce06bd6cbafdf9:3">=</span><span offset-key="63320f4f783e44658cce06bd6cbafdf9:4"> </span><span class="r-qtrn9a" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="63320f4f783e44658cce06bd6cbafdf9:5">"Hello "</span><span offset-key="63320f4f783e44658cce06bd6cbafdf9:6"> </span><span class="r-11faab8" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="63320f4f783e44658cce06bd6cbafdf9:7">+</span><span offset-key="63320f4f783e44658cce06bd6cbafdf9:8"> fname </span><span class="r-11faab8" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="63320f4f783e44658cce06bd6cbafdf9:9">+</span><span offset-key="63320f4f783e44658cce06bd6cbafdf9:10"> </span><span class="r-qtrn9a" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="63320f4f783e44658cce06bd6cbafdf9:11">" "</span><span offset-key="63320f4f783e44658cce06bd6cbafdf9:12"> </span><span class="r-11faab8" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="63320f4f783e44658cce06bd6cbafdf9:13">+</span><span offset-key="63320f4f783e44658cce06bd6cbafdf9:14"> lname</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="63320f4f783e44658cce06bd6cbafdf9:15">;</span></span>

Copied!

<span key="9d31b53208dd48918f68dc7c339e69fb">**Single expression arrow functions**</span>

<span key="25e11481c53848d6b08453650cb55ba0">**Reminder:**<span offset-key="25e11481c53848d6b08453650cb55ba0:1"> In JavaScript, an </span>*expression*<span offset-key="25e11481c53848d6b08453650cb55ba0:3"> is a line of code that returns a value. </span>*Statements*<span offset-key="25e11481c53848d6b08453650cb55ba0:5"> are, more generally, any line of code.</span></span>

<span key="c2ae8b58172943c4a72f0b9826baf057"><span offset-key="c2ae8b58172943c4a72f0b9826baf057:0">One of the most fun things about single expression arrow functions is they allow for something previously unavailable in JavaScript: </span>**implicit returns**<span offset-key="c2ae8b58172943c4a72f0b9826baf057:2">. Meaning, in an arrow function with a single-expression block, the curly braces (</span>`{ }`<span offset-key="c2ae8b58172943c4a72f0b9826baf057:4">) and the </span>`return`<span offset-key="c2ae8b58172943c4a72f0b9826baf057:6"> are keyword are </span>**implied**<span offset-key="c2ae8b58172943c4a72f0b9826baf057:8">.</span></span>

1

<span key="c0a87e2f54a44df4b9103997e39ec950"><span slate-leaf="true" offset-key="c0a87e2f54a44df4b9103997e39ec950:0">argument</span><span offset-key="c0a87e2f54a44df4b9103997e39ec950:1"> </span><span class="r-11faab8" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="c0a87e2f54a44df4b9103997e39ec950:2">=></span><span offset-key="c0a87e2f54a44df4b9103997e39ec950:3"> expression</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="c0a87e2f54a44df4b9103997e39ec950:4">;</span><span offset-key="c0a87e2f54a44df4b9103997e39ec950:5"> </span><span class="r-17y197c" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="c0a87e2f54a44df4b9103997e39ec950:6">// equal to (argument) => { return expression };</span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3NC05MTMyOF8iIGNsYXNzPSJyLWg3Z2RvYiByLTEwcHR1bjcgci0xdnppOHhpIiBzdHlsZT0id2lkdGg6MTZweCI+PHBhdGggZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBjbGlwLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGQ9Ik0wIC41QS41LjUgMCAwMS41IDBoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNVY0aC0xVjFIMXY5aDN2MUguNWEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUtLjVWLjV6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTUgNS41YS41LjUgMCAwMS41LS41aDEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS41LjV2MTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LjVoLTEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNXYtMTB6TTYgNnY5aDlWNkg2eiIgZmlsbD0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

Copied!

<span key="67f68eef8fc54d3280c46cfcfab1fcab"><span offset-key="67f68eef8fc54d3280c46cfcfab1fcab:0">Look at the below example you can see how we use this snazzy </span>*implicit returns*<span offset-key="67f68eef8fc54d3280c46cfcfab1fcab:2"> syntax:</span></span>

1

<span key="094088281aba492b8f63e7c7dcf3915b"><span class="r-y7gyvo" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="094088281aba492b8f63e7c7dcf3915b:0">const</span><span offset-key="094088281aba492b8f63e7c7dcf3915b:1"> </span><span slate-leaf="true" offset-key="094088281aba492b8f63e7c7dcf3915b:2">multiply</span><span offset-key="094088281aba492b8f63e7c7dcf3915b:3"> </span><span class="r-11faab8" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="094088281aba492b8f63e7c7dcf3915b:4">=</span><span offset-key="094088281aba492b8f63e7c7dcf3915b:5"> </span><span class="r-y7gyvo" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="094088281aba492b8f63e7c7dcf3915b:6">function</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="094088281aba492b8f63e7c7dcf3915b:7">(</span><span slate-leaf="true" offset-key="094088281aba492b8f63e7c7dcf3915b:8">num1</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="094088281aba492b8f63e7c7dcf3915b:9">,</span><span slate-leaf="true" offset-key="094088281aba492b8f63e7c7dcf3915b:10"> num2</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="094088281aba492b8f63e7c7dcf3915b:11">)</span><span offset-key="094088281aba492b8f63e7c7dcf3915b:12"> </span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="094088281aba492b8f63e7c7dcf3915b:13">{</span></span>

2

<span key="7adbe175a03a470684792d6139e8c0c9"><span offset-key="7adbe175a03a470684792d6139e8c0c9:0"> </span><span class="r-y7gyvo" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="7adbe175a03a470684792d6139e8c0c9:1">return</span><span offset-key="7adbe175a03a470684792d6139e8c0c9:2"> num1 </span><span class="r-11faab8" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="7adbe175a03a470684792d6139e8c0c9:3">\*</span><span offset-key="7adbe175a03a470684792d6139e8c0c9:4"> num2</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="7adbe175a03a470684792d6139e8c0c9:5">;</span></span>

3

<span key="e4a2ac60a3fd48d4876a95787dc7ba14"><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="e4a2ac60a3fd48d4876a95787dc7ba14:0">};</span></span>

4

<span key="6ae71e7c7acc4cc49ee666b98410fdb1"><span offset-key="6ae71e7c7acc4cc49ee666b98410fdb1:0"><span slate-zero-width="n">​</span></span></span>

<span key="c5ea0a63d55c4738a22da4f7d9f8129f"><span class="r-17y197c" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="c5ea0a63d55c4738a22da4f7d9f8129f:0">// do not need to explicitly state return!</span></span>

<span key="e8922482edd44e93a17220fc5f33304c"><span class="r-y7gyvo" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="e8922482edd44e93a17220fc5f33304c:0">const</span><span offset-key="e8922482edd44e93a17220fc5f33304c:1"> </span><span slate-leaf="true" offset-key="e8922482edd44e93a17220fc5f33304c:2">arrowMultiply</span><span offset-key="e8922482edd44e93a17220fc5f33304c:3"> </span><span class="r-11faab8" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="e8922482edd44e93a17220fc5f33304c:4">=</span><span offset-key="e8922482edd44e93a17220fc5f33304c:5"> </span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="e8922482edd44e93a17220fc5f33304c:6">(</span><span slate-leaf="true" offset-key="e8922482edd44e93a17220fc5f33304c:7">num1</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="e8922482edd44e93a17220fc5f33304c:8">,</span><span slate-leaf="true" offset-key="e8922482edd44e93a17220fc5f33304c:9"> num2</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="e8922482edd44e93a17220fc5f33304c:10">)</span><span offset-key="e8922482edd44e93a17220fc5f33304c:11"> </span><span class="r-11faab8" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="e8922482edd44e93a17220fc5f33304c:12">=></span><span offset-key="e8922482edd44e93a17220fc5f33304c:13"> num1 </span><span class="r-11faab8" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="e8922482edd44e93a17220fc5f33304c:14">\*</span><span offset-key="e8922482edd44e93a17220fc5f33304c:15"> num2</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="e8922482edd44e93a17220fc5f33304c:16">;</span></span>

<span key="bec62cd5035b47ff9d27d7b57fe9421b">**Syntactic ambiguity with arrow functions**</span>

<span key="09d88d30cbd94182b27fc39cdbadf4e5"><span offset-key="09d88d30cbd94182b27fc39cdbadf4e5:0">In Javascript, </span>`{}`<span offset-key="09d88d30cbd94182b27fc39cdbadf4e5:2"> can signify either an empty object or an empty block.</span></span>

1

<span key="9aea52e8d36f4466806491b65775f0bb"><span class="r-y7gyvo" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="9aea52e8d36f4466806491b65775f0bb:0">const</span><span offset-key="9aea52e8d36f4466806491b65775f0bb:1"> </span><span slate-leaf="true" offset-key="9aea52e8d36f4466806491b65775f0bb:2">ambiguousFunction</span><span offset-key="9aea52e8d36f4466806491b65775f0bb:3"> </span><span class="r-11faab8" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="9aea52e8d36f4466806491b65775f0bb:4">=</span><span offset-key="9aea52e8d36f4466806491b65775f0bb:5"> </span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="9aea52e8d36f4466806491b65775f0bb:6">()</span><span offset-key="9aea52e8d36f4466806491b65775f0bb:7"> </span><span class="r-11faab8" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="9aea52e8d36f4466806491b65775f0bb:8">=></span><span offset-key="9aea52e8d36f4466806491b65775f0bb:9"> </span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="9aea52e8d36f4466806491b65775f0bb:10">{};</span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3NC05MTMyOF8iIGNsYXNzPSJyLWg3Z2RvYiByLTEwcHR1bjcgci0xdnppOHhpIiBzdHlsZT0id2lkdGg6MTZweCI+PHBhdGggZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBjbGlwLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGQ9Ik0wIC41QS41LjUgMCAwMS41IDBoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNVY0aC0xVjFIMXY5aDN2MUguNWEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUtLjVWLjV6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTUgNS41YS41LjUgMCAwMS41LS41aDEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS41LjV2MTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LjVoLTEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNXYtMTB6TTYgNnY5aDlWNkg2eiIgZmlsbD0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

Copied!

<span key="231eb92a7f344076a762cc0f8ffdc4c9"><span offset-key="231eb92a7f344076a762cc0f8ffdc4c9:0">Is </span>`ambiguousFunction`<span offset-key="231eb92a7f344076a762cc0f8ffdc4c9:2"> supposed to return an empty object or an empty code block? Confusing right? JavaScript standards state that the curly braces after a fat arrow evaluate to an empty block (which has the default value of </span>`undefined`<span offset-key="231eb92a7f344076a762cc0f8ffdc4c9:4">):</span></span>

1

<span key="82ff0fdbf4b9400ab7a9d7684dee4743"><span slate-leaf="true" offset-key="82ff0fdbf4b9400ab7a9d7684dee4743:0">ambiguousFunction</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="82ff0fdbf4b9400ab7a9d7684dee4743:1">();</span><span offset-key="82ff0fdbf4b9400ab7a9d7684dee4743:2"> </span><span class="r-17y197c" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="82ff0fdbf4b9400ab7a9d7684dee4743:3">// undefined</span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3NC05MTMyOF8iIGNsYXNzPSJyLWg3Z2RvYiByLTEwcHR1bjcgci0xdnppOHhpIiBzdHlsZT0id2lkdGg6MTZweCI+PHBhdGggZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBjbGlwLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGQ9Ik0wIC41QS41LjUgMCAwMS41IDBoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNVY0aC0xVjFIMXY5aDN2MUguNWEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUtLjVWLjV6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTUgNS41YS41LjUgMCAwMS41LS41aDEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS41LjV2MTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LjVoLTEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNXYtMTB6TTYgNnY5aDlWNkg2eiIgZmlsbD0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

<span key="8c6df9868fc9449b8cab6c4759dc4a85"><span offset-key="8c6df9868fc9449b8cab6c4759dc4a85:0">To make a single-expression fat arrow return an empty object, wrap that object within parentheses:</span></span>

1

<span key="7d792c3d71994435af22c3660401b7ee"><span class="r-17y197c" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="7d792c3d71994435af22c3660401b7ee:0">// this will implicitly return an empty object</span></span>

2

<span key="01dac030237a4fa680b53d22bb7e31e1"><span class="r-y7gyvo" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="01dac030237a4fa680b53d22bb7e31e1:0">const</span><span offset-key="01dac030237a4fa680b53d22bb7e31e1:1"> </span><span slate-leaf="true" offset-key="01dac030237a4fa680b53d22bb7e31e1:2">clearFunction</span><span offset-key="01dac030237a4fa680b53d22bb7e31e1:3"> </span><span class="r-11faab8" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="01dac030237a4fa680b53d22bb7e31e1:4">=</span><span offset-key="01dac030237a4fa680b53d22bb7e31e1:5"> </span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="01dac030237a4fa680b53d22bb7e31e1:6">()</span><span offset-key="01dac030237a4fa680b53d22bb7e31e1:7"> </span><span class="r-11faab8" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="01dac030237a4fa680b53d22bb7e31e1:8">=></span><span offset-key="01dac030237a4fa680b53d22bb7e31e1:9"> </span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="01dac030237a4fa680b53d22bb7e31e1:10">({});</span></span>

<span key="6477ce8d29b64b619c40c6724b1e1f49">**Arrow functions are anonymous**</span>

<span key="8dba26b3d26744e08504aa5ccb0781b8"><span offset-key="8dba26b3d26744e08504aa5ccb0781b8:0">Fat arrows are </span>*anonymous*<span offset-key="8dba26b3d26744e08504aa5ccb0781b8:2">, like their </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Anonymous_function" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="60519f8b6f76433baf31276872cbe705" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-91324_259-91325-237__"><span data-key="49717678f8e74bceb653e652bc018d45"><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="49717678f8e74bceb653e652bc018d45:0">lambda</code></span></span></a><span key="112a1d9438ec4ccc819bc7431e385976"><span offset-key="112a1d9438ec4ccc819bc7431e385976:0"> counterparts in other languages.</span></span>

1

<span key="e2129cec27c84967893675ded556ca76"><span offset-key="e2129cec27c84967893675ded556ca76:0">That's about all you need to know for arrow functions syntax-wise. Arrow functions aren't just a different way of writing functions, though. They </span>*behave*<span offset-key="e2129cec27c84967893675ded556ca76:2"> differently too - especially when it comes to context!</span></span>

## 

<span key="7b0ab2ce05c74f4ab429132d155cddf7"><span offset-key="7b0ab2ce05c74f4ab429132d155cddf7:0">Arrow functions with context</span></span>

<span key="cd6856647f5c432482106091442190f6"><span offset-key="cd6856647f5c432482106091442190f6:0">Arrow functions, unlike normal functions, </span>**carry over context, binding** **`this`** **lexically**<span offset-key="cd6856647f5c432482106091442190f6:4">. In other words, </span>`this`<span offset-key="cd6856647f5c432482106091442190f6:6"> means the same thing inside an arrow function that it does outside of it. Unlike all other functions, the value of </span>`this`<span offset-key="cd6856647f5c432482106091442190f6:8"> inside an arrow function is not dependent on how it is invoked.</span></span>

<span key="91e31858a9634e6d8dc79db556ca9192"><span offset-key="91e31858a9634e6d8dc79db556ca9192:0">Let's do a little compare and contrast to illustrate this point:</span></span>

1

2

<span key="14fe65ec9031492ca2a15f1f8d3f96a7"><span slate-leaf="true" offset-key="14fe65ec9031492ca2a15f1f8d3f96a7:0">arrowName</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="14fe65ec9031492ca2a15f1f8d3f96a7:1">();</span><span offset-key="14fe65ec9031492ca2a15f1f8d3f96a7:2"> </span><span class="r-17y197c" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="14fe65ec9031492ca2a15f1f8d3f96a7:3">// The original object!</span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3NC05MTMyOF8iIGNsYXNzPSJyLWg3Z2RvYiByLTEwcHR1bjcgci0xdnppOHhpIiBzdHlsZT0id2lkdGg6MTZweCI+PHBhdGggZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBjbGlwLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGQ9Ik0wIC41QS41LjUgMCAwMS41IDBoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNVY0aC0xVjFIMXY5aDN2MUguNWEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUtLjVWLjV6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTUgNS41YS41LjUgMCAwMS41LS41aDEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS41LjV2MTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LjVoLTEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNXYtMTB6TTYgNnY5aDlWNkg2eiIgZmlsbD0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

Copied!

<span key="c7edfc4520ff415c9914971c9d8509ef"><span offset-key="c7edfc4520ff415c9914971c9d8509ef:0">Let's walk through what just happened - we created a </span>`testObj`<span offset-key="c7edfc4520ff415c9914971c9d8509ef:2"> with two methods that each returned an anonymous function. The difference between these two methods is that the </span>`createArrowFunc`<span offset-key="c7edfc4520ff415c9914971c9d8509ef:4"> function contained an arrow function inside it. When we invoked both methods we created two function - the </span>`noName`<span offset-key="c7edfc4520ff415c9914971c9d8509ef:6"> function creating it's own scope and context while the </span>`arrowName`<span offset-key="c7edfc4520ff415c9914971c9d8509ef:8"> </span>**kept**<span offset-key="c7edfc4520ff415c9914971c9d8509ef:10"> the context of the function that created it (</span>`createArrowFunc`<span offset-key="c7edfc4520ff415c9914971c9d8509ef:12">'s context of </span>`testObj`<span offset-key="c7edfc4520ff415c9914971c9d8509ef:14">).</span></span>

<span key="207a8bca7cbe4fadbf65afa487b6c17a"><span offset-key="207a8bca7cbe4fadbf65afa487b6c17a:0">An arrow function will always have the same context as the function that created it - giving it access to variables available in that context (like </span>`this.name`<span offset-key="207a8bca7cbe4fadbf65afa487b6c17a:2"> in this case!)</span></span>

### 

<span key="c8ac4f24340446758da8ea813a442251"><span offset-key="c8ac4f24340446758da8ea813a442251:0">No binding in arrow functions</span></span>

<span key="84ce502db7604d3dbf564e3aa2721076"><span offset-key="84ce502db7604d3dbf564e3aa2721076:0">One thing to know about arrow functions is since they already have a </span>*bound context*<span offset-key="84ce502db7604d3dbf564e3aa2721076:2">, unlike normal functions, you can't reassign </span>`this`<span offset-key="84ce502db7604d3dbf564e3aa2721076:4">. The </span>`this`<span offset-key="84ce502db7604d3dbf564e3aa2721076:6"> in arrow functions is always what it was at the time that the arrow function was declared.</span></span>

1

<span key="6e57485f1bc4450a9f23c2182ba74921"><span class="r-y7gyvo" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="6e57485f1bc4450a9f23c2182ba74921:0">const</span><span offset-key="6e57485f1bc4450a9f23c2182ba74921:1"> </span><span slate-leaf="true" offset-key="6e57485f1bc4450a9f23c2182ba74921:2">returnName</span><span offset-key="6e57485f1bc4450a9f23c2182ba74921:3"> </span><span class="r-11faab8" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="6e57485f1bc4450a9f23c2182ba74921:4">=</span><span offset-key="6e57485f1bc4450a9f23c2182ba74921:5"> </span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="6e57485f1bc4450a9f23c2182ba74921:6">()</span><span offset-key="6e57485f1bc4450a9f23c2182ba74921:7"> </span><span class="r-11faab8" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="6e57485f1bc4450a9f23c2182ba74921:8">=></span><span offset-key="6e57485f1bc4450a9f23c2182ba74921:9"> </span><span class="r-y7gyvo" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="6e57485f1bc4450a9f23c2182ba74921:10">this</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="6e57485f1bc4450a9f23c2182ba74921:11">.</span><span offset-key="6e57485f1bc4450a9f23c2182ba74921:12">name</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="6e57485f1bc4450a9f23c2182ba74921:13">;</span></span>

## 

<span key="0c946072e0df485b9620f79fd6c129ab"><span offset-key="0c946072e0df485b9620f79fd6c129ab:0">Scope Problems</span></span>

<span key="df3d539b5930445383974a0ff94277fd"><span offset-key="df3d539b5930445383974a0ff94277fd:0">It's time to get some practice using scope in the wild! This task includes a link to download a </span>`zip`<span offset-key="df3d539b5930445383974a0ff94277fd:2"> file with a number of problems.</span></span>

<span key="c661514add3c49cbad1e919fd3865287"><span offset-key="c661514add3c49cbad1e919fd3865287:0">Complete the problems in the order specified. In addition to the prompts available at the top of each file, Mocha specs are provided to test your work.</span></span>

<span key="0f267c6afb39419c9bbe339e7e3bf558"><span offset-key="0f267c6afb39419c9bbe339e7e3bf558:0">To get started, use the following commands:</span></span>

1.  <span class="r-1awozwy r-1nf4jbm r-6koalj r-18u37iz r-gg6oyi r-ubezar r-16dba41 r-135wba7 r-1m04atk r-1pyaxff" contenteditable="false" style="height:24px">1.</span>
    <span key="1a55fb8a1c7e43e99520d158fed50208">`cd`<span offset-key="1a55fb8a1c7e43e99520d158fed50208:1"> into the project directory</span></span>

2.  <span class="r-1awozwy r-1nf4jbm r-6koalj r-18u37iz r-gg6oyi r-ubezar r-16dba41 r-135wba7 r-1m04atk r-1pyaxff" contenteditable="false" style="height:24px">2.</span>
    <span key="a98e860fd86f41f0b58f07059a4950e8">`npm install`<span offset-key="a98e860fd86f41f0b58f07059a4950e8:1"> to install any dependencies</span></span>

3.  <span class="r-1awozwy r-1nf4jbm r-6koalj r-18u37iz r-gg6oyi r-ubezar r-16dba41 r-135wba7 r-1m04atk r-1pyaxff" contenteditable="false" style="height:24px">3.</span>
    <span key="3aa1db008f0a4dbf8db7a48989b9fe6e">`mocha`<span offset-key="3aa1db008f0a4dbf8db7a48989b9fe6e:1"> to run the test cases</span></span>

# 

<span key="ca29930232f24a5497f757aca41c9fc9"><span offset-key="ca29930232f24a5497f757aca41c9fc9:0">WhiteBoarding Problem</span></span>

<span key="9f4b7586bb2e4e9bba5031b4c300cf2d"><span offset-key="9f4b7586bb2e4e9bba5031b4c300cf2d:0">Write a function named </span>`hiddenCounter()`<span offset-key="9f4b7586bb2e4e9bba5031b4c300cf2d:2">. The </span>`hiddenCounter`<span offset-key="9f4b7586bb2e4e9bba5031b4c300cf2d:4"> function will start by declaring a variable that will keep track of a count and will be initially set to 0. Upon first invocation </span>`hiddenCounter`<span offset-key="9f4b7586bb2e4e9bba5031b4c300cf2d:6"> will return a function. Every subsequent invocation will increment the previously described count variable.</span></span>

<span key="9eb924d08ece471a9f8278f6c618fee8"><span offset-key="9eb924d08ece471a9f8278f6c618fee8:0">Explain how the closure you have created affects the scope of both functions.</span></span>

<span key="2e13b12ef16b449f9c8f2a6cf6dd14d5"><span offset-key="2e13b12ef16b449f9c8f2a6cf6dd14d5:0">Examples:</span></span>

1

<span key="0e5433d5eef5442f8e6d637efba4d8b0"><span class="r-y7gyvo" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="0e5433d5eef5442f8e6d637efba4d8b0:0">let</span><span offset-key="0e5433d5eef5442f8e6d637efba4d8b0:1"> hidden1 </span><span class="r-11faab8" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="0e5433d5eef5442f8e6d637efba4d8b0:2">=</span><span offset-key="0e5433d5eef5442f8e6d637efba4d8b0:3"> </span><span slate-leaf="true" offset-key="0e5433d5eef5442f8e6d637efba4d8b0:4">hiddenCounter</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="0e5433d5eef5442f8e6d637efba4d8b0:5">();</span><span offset-key="0e5433d5eef5442f8e6d637efba4d8b0:6"> </span><span class="r-17y197c" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="0e5433d5eef5442f8e6d637efba4d8b0:7">//returns a function</span></span>

2

<span key="06ddc15b1a954ff5b78e9a318af3d4c5"><span slate-leaf="true" offset-key="06ddc15b1a954ff5b78e9a318af3d4c5:0">hidden1</span><span class="r-dyg9za" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="06ddc15b1a954ff5b78e9a318af3d4c5:1">();</span><span offset-key="06ddc15b1a954ff5b78e9a318af3d4c5:2"> </span><span class="r-17y197c" slate-leaf="true" offset-key="06ddc15b1a954ff5b78e9a318af3d4c5:3">// returns 1</span></span>

3
